[Archive link](https://list.indology.info/pipermail/indology/2024-February/058786.html)

The requested text seems not to be available there.

I have on my computer a file for Thirteen Principal Upaniṣads, including the requested text, typed by the late Muneo Tokunaga in 1989. It contains the phrase "The copyright of this text belongs to M.T. Duplication of the text allowed only under agreement." But since he has generously made public so many other e-texts, I suppose he wouldn't have minded this one being shared. So here it is. The transcription scheme has not yet been normalized but I am sure some clever colleague can help with this.

May I go off topic and ask if anyone knows whether there is any hope that GRETIL can become active again, or whether some alternative cumulative repository can be set up? Olliver Hellwig's recent announcement of an e-text on his own github platform shows that we really need a community-based solution.

Best wishes,

Arlo Griffiths

Dear all,

I am looking for a digitally-searchable version of the Maitrī Upaniṣad, aka Maitrāyaṇīya, etc. Does anyone have any leads?

With thanks,
Cicely Bonnin

<īśa upanisad>(IU)
īśā vāsyam idam sarvam yat kimca jagati.ām jagat / tena tyakta3na bhunjīthā[\bhuj.prp] mā gr̥dhah[\gr̥dh] kasya svid dhanam (īū1)
kurvann[\kr̥] eva^iha karmāni jijīviset[\jiḍesid] śatam samāh / evam tvayi na^anyathā^itas'asti na karma \lipyate nara7 (īū2)
asuryā nāma te lokā andha3na tamasā^āvr̥tāh / tāms te pretya[pra\i.g]^abhigacchanti[abhi\gam] ye ke ca^ātmaḥanas^janāh (īū3)
anejad[\ej.prp] ekam manaso javīyas^na^enad devā āpnuvan[\āp.ipf] pūrvam arsat[\r̥s.ipf?] / tad dhāvatas[\dhāv.prp]'anyān atyeti[ati\i] tisthat[\sthā.prp] tasminn apas^mātariśvā dadhāti[\dhā] (īū4)
tad ejati[\ej] tan na^ejati[\ej] tad dūra7 tad^u^antika7 / tad antarasya sarvasya tad u sarvasya^asya bāhyatah (īū5)
yas tu sarvāni bhūtāni ātmani^eva^anupaśyati[anu\paś] / sarva.bhūta7su ca^ātmānam tato na vijugupsate[\gupḍesid] (īū6) [atm]
yasmin sarvāni bhūtāni ātmā^eva^abhūd[\bhū.aor] vijānatah / tatra kas^mohah kah śoka ekatvam anupaśatah[anu\paś.prp] (īū7)
sa paryagāt[pari\gā.aor] śukram akāyam avranam asnāviram śuddham apāpa.viddham / kavir manīsī paribhūh svayam.bhūr yāthātathyatas'arthān vyadadhāt[vi\dhā.aor]^śāśvatībhyah samābhyah (īū8)
andham tamas2 praviśanti[pra\viś] ye avidyām upāsate[upa\ās] / tatas^bhūyas^iva te tamas2 ya u vidyāyām ratāh (īū9)
anyad eva^āhur[\āh.pf] vidyayā anyad āhur[\āh.pf] avidyayā / iti śuśruma[\śru.pf] dhīrānām ye nas tad vicacaksire[vi\caks.pf] (īū10)
vidyām ca^avidyām ca yas tad veda[\vid.pf]^ubhayam saha / avidyayā mr̥tyum tīrtvā[\tr̥r̥.g] vidyayā^amr̥tam aśnute[\aś] (īū11)
andham tamas2 praviśanti[pra\viś] ye'asambhūtim upāsate[upa\ās] / tatas^bhūyas^iva te tamas2 ya u sambhūti.ām ratāh (īū12)
anyad eva^āhuh[\āh.pf] sambhavād anyad āhur[\āh.pf] asambhavāt / iti śuśruma[\śru.pf] dhīrānām ye nas tad vicacaksire[vi\caks.pf] (īū13)
(a)sambhūtim ca vināśam ca yas tad veda[\vid.pf]^ubhayam saha / vināśa3na mr̥tyum tīrtvā[\tr̥r̥.g]^(a)sambhūti.ā^amr̥tam aśnute[\aś] (īū14)
hiranmaya3na pātra3na satyasya^apihita[api\dhā.pp] sukham / tattvam pūsann apāvr̥nu[apā\vr̥.ipf] satyaḍharmāya dr̥staye[dr̥sti] (īū15)
pūsann ekaṛ̥si8 yama sūrya prājāpatya vyūha raśmīn samūha[sam\ūh.ipf] / tejas^yat te rūpam kalyānatamam tat te paśyāmi[\paś] yas^asāv asau purusah so^aham asmi[\as] (īū16)
vāyur anilam amr̥tam atha^idam bhasma.antam śarīram / om kratu8 smara[\smr̥.ipf] kr̥tam smara[\smr̥.ipv] kratu8 smara[\smr̥.ipv] kr̥tam smara[\smr̥.ipv] (īū17)
agni8 naya[\nī.ipv] supathā rāye[rai] asmān viśvāni deva vayunāni vidvat1m / yuyodhi[\yu.pf.ipv] asmat^juhurānam[\hvr̥.pf.ppl] enas^bhūyisthām te nama.uktim vidhema[vi\dhā.opt] (īū18) =End of īū=


<āitareya ūpanisad>(āū)
om ātmā vā idam eka eva^agra āsīt[\as.ipf] / na^anyat kimcana misat[\mis.a-less.ipf] / sa īksata[\īks.a-less.ipf] lokān nu sr̥jā[\sr̥j.prṣubj] iti (āū1.1)
sa imāml lokān asr̥jata[\sr̥j.ipf] / ambhas^marīcīr maram āpas^ambhah para3na divam dyauh pratisthā^antariksam marīci1p / pr̥thivī maras^yā adhastāt tā āpas. (āū1.2)
sa īksata[\īks.a-less.ipf]^ime nu lokā loka.pālān nu sr̥jā[sr̥j.prṣubj] iti / so^ap.bhya eva purusam samuddhr̥tya[samut\dhr̥.g]^amūrchayat[\mūrch.caus.ipf] (āū1.3)
tam abhyatapat[abhi\tap.ipf] tasya^abhitaptasya mukham nirabhidyata[nis\bhid.ipf] yathā^andam (āū1.4a)
mukhād vāc^vācas'agnir nāsika1d nirabhidyetām[nis\bhid.ipf] (āū1.4b)
nāsikābhyām prānah prānād vāyur aksinī nirabhyetām[nis\bhid.ipf] (āū1.4c)
aksibhyām caksus^caksusa ādityah karnau nirabhidyetām[nis\bhid.ipf] (āū1.4d)
karnābhyām śrotram śrotrād diśas tvac^nirabhidyata[nis\bhid.ipf] (āū1.e)
tvaco lomāni lomabhya osadhi.vanaspati1p hr̥dayam nirabhidyata[nis\bhid.ipf] (āū1.4f)
hr̥dayāt^manas^manasaś candramā nābhir nirabhidyata[nis\bhid.ipf] (āū1.4g)
nābhi.ā apānas'apānād mr̥tyuh śiśnam nirabhidyata[nis\bhid.ipf] (āū1.4h)
śiśnād retas^retasa āpas. (āū1.4i)

tā etā devatāh sr̥stā asmin mahaty arnava7 prāpatams[pra\pat.ipf] tam aśanā.pipāsābhyām anvavārjat[anvava\arj.ipf] / (āū2.1a)
tā enam abruvan[\brū.ipf] āyatanam nah prajānīhi[pra\jnā.ipv] yasmin pratisthitā annam adāma[\adṣubj]^iti (āū2.1b)
tābhyas^gām ānayat[ā\nī.ipf] tā abruvan[\brū.ipf] na vai nas'ayam alam iti ) tābhyas^aśvam ānayat[ā\nī.ipf] tā abruvan[\brū.ipf] na vai nas'ayam alam iti (āū2.2)
tābhyah purusam ānayat[ā\nī.ipf] tā abruvan[\brū.ipf] sukr̥tam bata^iti purusas^vāva sukr̥tam (āū2.3a)
sā abravīd[\brū.ipf] yathā.āyatanam praviśata[pra\viś.ipv]^iti (āū2.3b)
agnir vāc^bhūtvā[\bhū.g] mukham prāviśad[pra\viś.ipf] vāyuh prānas^bhūtvā nāsike prāviśad[pra\viś.ipf] (āū2.4a)
ādityaś caksus^bhūtvā^aksinī prāviśad[pra\viś.ipf] diśah śrotram bhūtvā karnau praviśan[pra\viś.ipf] (āū2.4b)
osadhi.vanaspati1p lomāni bhūtvā tvacam prāviśamś[pra\viś.ipf] candramā manas^bhūtvā hr̥dayam prāviśan[pra\viś] (āū2.4c)
mr̥tyur apānas^bhūtvā nābhim prāviśad[pra\viś] āpas^retas^bhūtvā śiśnam prāviśan[pra\viś] (āū2.4d)
tam aśanā.pipāsā1d abrūtām[\brū.ipf] āvābhyām abhiprajānāi[\abhipra.jnā.ipv]^iti (āū2.5a)
te abravīd[\brū] etāsv eva vām devatāsv ābhajāmy[ā\bhaj] etāsu ghanini.au karomi[\kr̥]^iti / (āū2.5b)
tasmād yasmai kasyai ca devatāyai havis^gr̥hyate bhāgini.āv^eva^asyām aśanā.pipāsā1d bhavatah[\bhū] (āū2.5c)

sa īksata[\īks]^ime nu lokāś ca loka.pālāś ca^annam ebhyah sr̥jā[\sr̥j] iti (āū3.1)
so^apas'abhyatapat[abhi\tap] tābhyas^abhitaptābhyas^mūrtir ajāyata[\jan] yā vai sā mūrtir ajāyata[\jan]^annam vai tat (āū3.2)
tad enat sr̥stam parān atyajighāmsat[ati\han] tad vācā^ajighr̥ksat[\grah] tat^na^aśaknod[\śak] vācā grahītum[\grah] (āū3.3a)
sa yadd ha^enad vācā^agrahaisyad[\grah] abhivyāhr̥tya[abhivyā\hr̥] ha^eva^annam atrapsyat[\trap] (āū3.3b)
tat prāna3na^ajighr̥ksat[\grah] tat^na^aśaknot[\śak] prāna3na grahītum[\grah] sa yad dha^enat prāna3na^agrahaisyad[\grah] ābhiprānya ha^eva^annam atrapsyat[\tr̥p] (āū3.4)
tac caksusā^ajighr̥ksat[\grah] tan^na^aśaknot[\śak]^caksusā grahītum[\grah] sa yadd ha^enat^caksusā^agrahaisyad dr̥stvā ha^eva^annam atrapsyat[\tr̥p] (āū3.5)
tac śrotra3na^ajighr̥ksat[\grah] tan^na^aśaknot[\śak]^śrotra3na grahītum[\grah] sa yadd ha^enat^śrotra3na^agrahaisyad dr̥stvā ha^eva^annam atrapsyat[\tr̥p] (āū3.5)
tac śrotra3na^ajighr̥ksat[\grah] tan^na^aśaknot[\śak]^śrotra3na grahītum[\grah] sa yadd ha^enat^śrotra3na^agrahaisyat^śrutvā[\śru] ha^eva^annam atrapsyat[\tr̥p] (āū3.6)
tac tvacā^ajighr̥ksat[\grah] tan^na^aśaknot[\śak] tvacā grahītum[\grah] sa yadd ha^enat tvacā^agrahaisyat spr̥stvā[\spr̥ś] ha^eva^annam atrapsyat[\tr̥p] (āū3.7)
tan manasā^ajighr̥ksat[\grah] tan na^aśaknot[\śak]^manasā grahītum sa yadd ha^enat^manasā^agrahaisyad dhyātvā[\dhyā] ha^eva^annam atrapsyat[\tr̥p] (āū3.8)
tat^śiśna3na^ajighr̥ksat[\grah] tat^na^aśaknot[\śak]^śiśna3na grahītum[\grah] sa yadd ha^enat^śiśna3na^agrahaisyad[\grah] visr̥jya[vi\sr̥j] ha^eva^annam atrapsyat (āū3.9)
tad apāna3na^ajighr̥ksat[\grah] tad āvayat[\av] sā^esas[sa esas?]'annasya grahas^yad vāyur annāyur vā esa yad vāyuh (āū3.10)

sa īksata[\īks] katham nu^idam matṛ̥te syād[\as] iti sa īksata[\īks] katara3na prapadyā[pra\pad] iti (āū3.11a)
sa īksata[\īks] yadi vācā^abhivyāhr̥tam[abhivyā\hr̥] yadi prāna3na^abhiprānitam[abhipra\an] yadi caksusā dr̥stam[\dr̥ś] yadi śrotra3na śrutam[\śru] yadi tvacā spr̥stam[\spr̥ś] yadi manasā dhyātam[\dhyā] yadi^apāna3na^abhyapānitam[abhyapa\an] yadi śiśna3na visr̥stam[vi\sr̥j] atha kas'aham iti (āū3.11b)
sa etam eva sīmānam vidārya[vi\dr̥r̥]^etayā dvārā prāpadyata[pra\pad] (āū3.12a)
sā^esā vidr̥tir nāma dvās tad etat^nāndanam (āū3.12b)
tasya traya āvasathās trayah svapnā (āū3.12c)
ayam āvasathas'ayam āvasathas'ayam āvasatha iti (āū3.12d)
sa jātas^bhūtāny abhivyaikhyat[abhivyā\khyā] kim iha^anyam vā^avadisad[\vad] iti (āū3.13a)
sa etam eva purusam brahmma tatamam apaśyad[\paś] idam adarśam[? \dr̥ś] iti. (āū3.13b)
tasmād idamdras^nāma^idamdras^ha vai nāma tam idamdram santam indra ity ācaksate[ā\caks] paroksa3na. (āū3.14a)
paroksa.priyā iva hi devāh paroksa.priyā iva hi devāh. (āū3.14b)

purusa7 ha vā ayam āditas^garbhas^bhavati[\bhū] (āū4.1a)
yad etad retas^tad etat sarva5bhyas^anga5bhyas tejas^sambhūtam, ātmani^eva^ātmānam bibharti[\bhr̥] (āū4.1b) [atm]
tad yadā striyām simcaty[\sinc] atha^enat^janayati. tad asya prathamam janma. (āū4.1)
tat striyā ātma.bhūyam gacchati[\gam] yathā svam angam tathā (āū4.2a)
tasmād enām na hinasti[\hims] sā^asya^etam ātmānam atra gatam bhāvayati[\bhū] (āū4.2b) [atm]
sā bhāvayitrī bhāvayitavyā bhavati. (āū4.3a)
tam strī garbham bibharti[\bhr̥], so^agra eva kumāram janmanas'agra7'adhibhāvayati[adhi\bhū]. (āū4.3b)
yat kumāram janmanas'agra7'adhibhāvayaty[adhi\bhū] ātmānam eva tad bhāvayaty esām lokānām samsati.ā hi^ime lokās, tad asya dvitīyam janma. (āū4.3c)
so^asya^ayam ātmā punya5bhyah karmabhyah pratidhīyate[prati\dhā] (āū4.4a)
atha^asya^ayam itara ātmā kr̥ta.kr̥tyas^vayas.gatah praiti (āū4.4b)
sa itah prayann[pra\i] eva punar jāyate[\jan] tad asya tr̥tīyam janma (āū4.4c)
tad uktam r̥sinā -- garbha7 nu sann anvesām avedam[\vid] aham devānām janimāni viśvā (āū4.5a)
śatam mā pura āyasīr araksann[\raks] andhah[adha?] śyenas^javasā niradīyam[nis\dī'fly'] (āū4.5b)
iti garbha eva^enat^śayānas[\śī]^vāmadeva evam uvāca[\vac] (āū4.5c)
sa evam vidvat1m asmāt^śarīra.bhedād ūrdhva utkramya[ut\kram]^amusmint svarga7 loka7 sarvān kāmān āptvā[\āp]^amr̥tah samabhavat[sam\bhū] samabhavati[sam\bhū] (āū4.6)

kas'ayam ātmā^iti vayam upāsmahe[upa\ās] (āū5.1a)
katarah sa ātmā yena vā paśyati[\paś] yena vā śr̥noti[\śru] yena vā gandhān ājighrati[ā\ghrā] yena vā vācam vyākaroti[vyā\kr̥] yena vā svādu ca^asvādu ca vijānāti[vi\jnā] (āū5.1b)
yad etadd hr̥dayam manas^ca^etat / samjnānam ājnānam vijnānam prajnānam medhā dr̥stir - (āū5.2a)
matir manīsā jūtih smr̥tih samkalpah kratur asuh kāmas^vaśa iti (āū5.2b)
sarvāny eva^etāni prajnānasya nāmadheyāni bhavanti[\bhū] (āū5.2c)
esa brahmā^esa indra esa prajāpatir ete sarva1p devā imāni ca panca mahā.bhūtāni pr̥thivī vāyur ākāśa āpas^jyotīmsi^ity (āū5.3a)
etāni^imāni ca ksudraṃiśrāni^iva bījāni^itarāni ca^itarāni ca^andajāni ca jārujāni ca svedajāni ca^udbhijāni ca - (āū5.3b)
aśvā gāvah[go] purusā hastinas^yat kimca^idam prāni jangamam ca patatri ca yat^ca sthāvaram - (āū5.3c)
sarvam tat prajnāṇetram prajnāna7 pratisthitam[prati\sthā] prajnāṇetras^lokah prajnā pratisthā prajnānam brahma (āū5.3d)
sa etena prajna3na^ātmanā^asmāl lokād utkramya[ut\kram]^amusmin svarga7 loka7 sarvān kāmān āptvā[\āp]^amr̥tah samabhavat[sam\bhū] samabhavat[sam\bhū] (āū5.4) [atm]
om vāc^me manasi pratisthitā manas^me vāci pratisthitam āvir āvīr ma edhi vedasya ma ānīsthah - (āū6)
śrutam me mā prahāsīr[pra\hā] anena^adhīta3na^ahorātrān samdadhāmy[sam\dhā] - (āū6)
r̥tam vadisyāmi[\vad] satyam vadisyāmi[\vad] tan mām avatu[\av] tad uktāram avatv[\av] avatu[\av] mām avatu[\av] vaktāram[vaktr̥]  avatu vaktāram (āū6a)
śāntih śāntih śāntih (āū6b) =End of āitareya ūpanisad=


<Kāthaka ūpanisad>(Kathū)
(KathUp 0.0) namas^bhagavate vaivasvatāya mr̥tyu4 brahma.vidyā.ācāryāya naciketase ca (Kathū.introd)
(KathUp 1.1) om uśan[\vaś] ha vai vājaśravasah sarvavedasam dadau[\dā] / tasya ha naciketas1 nāma putra āsa[\as]
(KathUp 1.2) tam ha kumāram santam[\as] daksināsu nīyamānāsu[\nī] śraddhā^āviveśa[ā\viś] so^amanyata[\man]
(KathUp 1.2)
pīta.udakā jagdhaṭr̥nā[\jah] dugdhaḍohā[\duh] nirindriyāh / anandā nāma te lokās tān sa gacchati[\gam] tā dadat[\dā] (Kathū1.3)
sa ha^uvāca[\vac] pitaram tata kasmai mām dāsyasi[\dā]^iti / dvitīyam tr̥tīyam tam ha^uvāca[\vac] mr̥tyu4 tvā dadāmi[\dā]^iti (Kathū1.4)
bahūnām emi[\i] prathamas^bahūnām emi[\i] madhyamah / kimsvid yamasya kartavyam yat^mayā^adya karisyati[\kr̥] (Kathū1.5)
anupaśya[anu\paś] yathā pūrve pratipaśya[prati\paś] tathā^apare / sasyam iva martyah pacyate[\pac] sasyam iva^ājāyate[ā\jan] punah (Kathū1.6)
vaiśvānarah praviśati[pra\viś] atithir brāhmanas^gr̥hān / tasya^etām śāntim kurvanti[\kr̥] hara[\hr̥] vaivasvata.udakam (Kathū1.7)
āśā.pratīksā2d samgatam sūnr̥tām cestā.pūrta2d putra.paśūmś ca sarvān / etat vr̥nkte[\vr̥j] purusasya^alpaṃedhaso yasya^anaśnan[\aś] vasati[\vas] brāhmanas^gr̥ha7 (Kathū1.8)
tisras^rātrīr yad avātsīr[\vas] gr̥ha7 me'anaśnan[\aś] brahmann atithir namasyah / namas te'astu brahman svasti me'astu[\as] tasmāt prati trīn varān vr̥nīsva[\vr̥] (Kathū1.9)
śāntaṣamkalpah sumanas1 yathā syād[\as] vītaṃanyur gautamas^mā^abhi mr̥tyu8 / tvat.prasr̥stam[pra\sr̥j] mā^abhivadet[abhi\vad] prīta etat trayānām prathamam varam vr̥ne[\vr̥] (Kathū1.10)
yathā purastād bhavitā[\bhū] pratīta auddālakir ārunir mat.prasr̥stah[pra\sr̥j] / sukham rātrīh śayita[\śī] vītaṃanyus tvām dadr̥śivān[\dr̥ś] mr̥tyuṃukhāt pramuktam (Kathū1.11)
svarga7 loka7 na bhayam kimcana^asti[\as] na tatra tvam jarayā bibheti[\bhī] / ubhe tīrtvā[\tr̥r̥]^aśanāyā.pipāsā2d śoka.atigas^ modate[\mud] svarga.loka7 (Kathū1.12)
sa tam agnim svargyam adhyesi[adhi\i] mr̥tyu8 prabrūhi[pra\brū] tam śraddadhānāya mahyam / svarga.lokā amr̥tatvam bhajanta[\bhaj] etat dvitīya3na vr̥ne[\vr̥] vara3na (Kathū1.13)
pra te bravīmi[pra\brū] tad u me nibodha[ni\budh] svargyam agnim naciketas8 prajānan[pra\jnā] / ananta.loka.āptim atho pratisthām viddhi tvam etam nihitam guhāyām (Kathū1.14)
loka.ādim agnim tam uvāca[\vac] tasmai yā istakā yāvatīr vā yathā vā / sa ca^api tat pratyavadad[prati\vad] yathā.uktam atha^asya mr̥tyuih punar eva^āha[\ah] tustah (Kathū1.15)
tam abravīt[\brū] prīyamānas^mahā.ātmā varam tava^iha^adya dadāmi[\dā] bhūyas1 / tava^eva nāmnā[nāman] bhavitā[\bhū]^ayam agnih sr̥nkām ca^imām anekar̥ūpām gr̥hāna[\grah] (Kathū1.16)
triṇāciketas tribhir etya[\i] samdhim tri.karma.kr̥t tarati[\tr̥r̥] janmaṃr̥tyū / brahmaja.jnam devam īdyam viditvā[\vid] nicāyya[ni\ci]^imām śāntim atyantam eti[\i] (Kathū1.17)
triṇāciketas trayam etad viditvā[\vid] ya evam vidvāmś cinute[\ci] nāciketam / sa mr̥tyu.pāśān puratah pranodya[pra\nud] śoka.atigas^modate[\mud] svarga.loka7 (Kathū1.18)
esa te'agnir naciketah svargyas^yam avr̥nīthā[\vr̥] dvitīya3na vara3na / etam agnim tava^eva pravaksyanti[pra\vac] janāsas tr̥itīyam varam naciketas8 vr̥nīsva[\vr̥] (Kathū1.19)
yā^iyam preta7 vicikitsā manusya7'asti[\as]^ity eke na^ayam asti[\as]^iti ca^eke / etad vidyām[\vid] anuśistas tvayā^aham varānām esa varas tr̥tīyah (Kathū1.20)
devair atra^api vicikitsā purā na hi suvijneyam anur esa dharmah / anyam varam naciketas8 vr̥nīsva[\vr̥] mā mā^uparotsīr[upa\rudh] ati ma sr̥ja[ati\sr̥j]^enam (Kathū1.21)
devair atra^api vicikitsitam kila tvam ca mr̥tyu8 yat^na sujneyam ātha[\ah] / vaktr̥1 ca^asya tvāḍr̥ś^anyas^na labhyas^varas tulya etasya kaścit (Kathū1.22)
śata.āyusah putra.pautrān vr̥nīsva[\vr̥] bahūn paśūn hastiḥiranyam aśvān / bhūmi6 mahad. āyatanam vr̥nīsva[\vr̥] svayam ca jīva[\jiv] śaradas^yāvad icchasi[\is1] (Kathū1.23)
etat tulyam yadi \manyase varam \vr̥nīsva vittam cira.jīvikām ca / mahā.bhūmas^naciketas^tvam edhi[\as] kāmānām tvā kāma.bhājam karomi[\kr̥] (Kathū1.24)
ye ye kāmā durlabhā martya.loka7 sarvān kāmāmś chandatah[\chand] prārthayasva[pra\arth] (Kathū1.25a)
imā rāmāh sarathāh satūryā na hi^īdr̥śā lambhanīyā manusyaih (Kathū1.25b)
ābhir mat.prattābhih[pra\dā] paricārayasva[pari\car] naciketas^maranam mā^anuprāksīh[anu\prach] (Kathū1.25)
śvas.bhāvā martyasya yad antaka^etat sarva.indriyānām jarayanti[\jr̥r̥] tejas2 / api sarvam jīvitam alpam eva tava^eva vāhās tava nr̥tya.gītā1d (Kathū1.26)
na vitta3na tarpanīyas^manusyas^lapsyāmahe[\labh] vittam adrāksma[\dr̥ś] cet tvā / jīvisyāmas[\jiv]^yāvad īśisyasi[\īś] tvam varas tu me varanīyah sa eva (Kathū1.27)
ajīryatām[\jr̥r̥] amr̥tānām upetya[\upa\i] jīryan[\jr̥r̥] martyah kvadhasṣthah prajānan[pra\jnā] / abhidhyāyan[abhi\dhyā] varnar̥ati.pramodān atidīrgha7 jīvita7 kas^rameta[\ram] (Kathū1.28)
yasminn idam vicikitsanti[\cid] mr̥tyu7 yat sāmparāya7 mahati brūhi[\brū] nas tat / yas^ayam varas^gūdham anupravistas^na^anyam tasmāt^naciketas1 vr̥nīte[\vr̥] (Kathū1.29)

anyat^śreyas^anyad uta^eva preyas te ubhe nānā.artha1d purusam sinītah[\sā] / tayor śreyas^ādadānasya[ā\dā] sādhu bhavati[\bhū] hīyate[\hā]'arthād ya u preyas^vr̥nīte[\vr̥] (Kathū2.1)
śreyas^ca preyas^ca manusyam etas[\i] tau samparītya[sampari\i] vivinakti[vi\vij] dhīrah / śreyas^hi dhīras^abhi preyaso vr̥nīte[\vr̥] preyas^mandas^yoga.ksemāt vr̥nīte[\vr̥] (Kathū2.2)
sa tvam priyān priyar̥ūpāmś ca kāmān abhidhyāyan[abhi\dhyā] naciketas'atyasrāksīh[ati\sr̥j] / na^etām sr̥nkām vittamayīm[\i] avāptas^yasyām majjanti[\majj] bahu1p manusyāh (Kathū2.3)
dūram ete viparīta1d visūcī avidyā yā ca vidyā^iti jnātā / vidyā.abhīpsinam naciketasam manye[\man] na tvā kāmā bahu1p'alolupanta[\lup] (Kathū2.4)
avidyāyām antara7 vartamānāh svayamḍhīrāh panditamṃanyamānāh / damdramyamānāh[\dram] pariyanti[pari\i] mūdhā andha3na^eva nīyamānā[\nī] yathā^andhāh (Kathū2.5)
na sāmparāyah pratibhāti[prati\bhā] bālam pramādyantam[pra\mad] vittaṃoha3na mūudham / ayam lokas^na^asti para iti mānin1 punah punar vaśam āpadyate[ā\pad] me (Kathū2.6)
śravanāya^api bahubhir yo na labhyah śr̥nvantas'api bahu1p yam na vidyuh[\vid] / āścaryas^vaktr̥1 kuśalas'asya labhdr̥1'āścaryas jnātr̥1 kuśala.anuśistah (Kathū2.7)
na nara3na^avara3na prokta esa suvijneyas^bahudhā cintyamānah[\cint] / ananya.prokta7 gatir atra na^asti anīyas1m hy atarkyam anu.pramānāt (Kathū2.8)
jānāmy[\jnā] aham śevadhir ity anityam na hy adhruvaih prāpyate[pra\āp] hi dhruvam tat / tato mayā nāciketaś citas'agnir anityair dravyaih prāptavān[pra\āp] asmi nityam (Kathū2.10)
kāmasya^āptim jagatah pratisthām kratu6 anantyam abhayasya pāram / stomaṃahad.uru.gāyam pratisthām dr̥stvā[\dr̥ś] dhr̥ti.ā dhīras^naciketas'atyasrāksīh[ati\sr̥j] (Kathū2.11)
tam durdarśam gūdham anupravistam guhāḥitam gahvareṣtham purānam / adhyātma.yoga.adhigama3na devam matvā[\man] dhīras^harsa.śokau jahāti[\hā](Kathū2.12)[atm]
etat^śrutvā[\śru] samparigr̥hya[sampari\grah] martyah pravr̥hya[pra\vr̥j] dharmyam anum etam āpya[\āp] / sa modate[\mud] modanīyam hi labdhvā[\labh] vivr̥tam sadma naciketasam manye[\man] (Kathū2.13)
anyatra dharmād anyatra^adharmād anyata^asmāt kr̥ta.akr̥tāt / anyatra bhūtāt^ca bhavyāt^ca yat tat \paśyasi tad \vada (Kathū2.14)
sarva1p vedā yat padam āmananti[ā\man] tapas2p sarvāni ca yad \vadanti / yad icchantas^[\is1] brahmacaryam caranti[\car] tat te padam samgraha3na bravīmy[\brū] om ity etat (Kathū2.15)
etad dhy eva^aksaram brahma etad dhy eva^aksaram param / etad dhy eva^aksaram jnātvā yas^yad icchati[\is1] tasya tat (Kathū2.16)
etad ālambanam śrestham etad ālambanam param / etad ālambanam jnātvā[\jnā] brahma.loka7 \mahīyate (Kathū2.17)
na jāyate[\jan] mriyate[\mr̥] vā vipaścit^na^ayam kutaścit^na babhūva[\bhū] kaścit / ajas^nityah śāśvatās'ayam purānas^na \hanyate \hanyamāna7 śarīra7 (Kathū2.18)
hantr̥1 cet^\manyate hantum hataś cet \manyate hatam / ubhau tau na vijānītas[vi\jnā]^na^ayam \hanti na \hanyate (Kathū2.19)
anu5 anīyas1m mahatas^mahīyas1m ātmā^asya jantu6 nihitas^guhāyām / tam akratuh \paśyati vīta.śokas^dhātu.prasādāt^mahimānam ātmanah (Kathū2.20)
āsīnas[ā\sad]^dūram \vrajati śayānas[\śī]^\yāti sarvatah / kas tam mada.amadam devam madanyas^\nātum \arhati (Kathū2.21)
aśarīram śarīra7sv anavastha7sv avasthitam / mahāntam vibhum ātmānam matvā dhīras^na śocati[\śuc] (Kathū2.22)
na^ayam ātmā pravacana3na labhyas^na medhayā na bahunā śuruta3na /yam eva^esa \r̥nute tena labhyas tasya^esa ātmā vivr̥nute[vi\vr̥] tanūm svām (Kathū2.23)
na^aviratas^duścaritāt^na^aśāntas^na^asamāhitah / na^aśāntaṃānasas^vā^api prajnāna3na^enam \āpnuyāt (Kathū2.24)
yasya brahma ca ksatram ca ubhe bhavata odanah / mr̥tyur yasya^upasecanam ka itthā veda[\vid] yatra sah (Kathū2.25)
r̥tam pibantau[\pā] sukr̥tasya loka7 guhām pravistau parama7 para.ardha7 / chāyāṭapa2d brahma.vidas^\vadanti panca.agni1p ye ca triṇāciketāh (Kathū3.1)
yah setur ījānānām[\yaj] aksaram brahma yat param / abhayam titīrsatām[\tr̥r̥] pāram nāciketam \śakemahi (Kathū3.2)
ātmānam rathinam \viddhi śarīram ratham eva tu / buddhim tu sārathim viddhi manas^pragraham eva ca (Kathū3.3)
indriyāni hayān āhur[\ah] visayāms tesu gocarān / ātma.indriyaṃanas.yuktam bhoktr̥1 ^ity āhur[\ah] manīsinah (Kathū3.4)
yas tv avijnānavān bhavaty[\bhū] ayukta3na manasā sadā / tasya^indriyāny avaśyāni dusta.aśvā iva sārathi6 (Kathū3.5)
yas tu vijnānavān bhavati[\bhū] yukta3na manasā sadā / tasya^indriyāni vaśyāni sat.aśvā iva sārathi7 (Kathū3.6)
yas tv avijnānavān bhavaty[\bhū] amanaskah sadā^aśucih / na sa tat padam \āpnoti samsāram ca^adhigacchati[adhi\gam] (Kathū3.7)
yas tu vijnānavān bhavati[\bhū] samanaskah sadā śucih / sa tu tat padam \āpnoti yasmād bhūyas^na jāyate[\jan] (Kathū3.8)
vijnānaṣārathir yas tu manas.pragrahavān narah / so^adhvanah pāram \āpnoti tad visnu6 paramam padam (Kathū3.9)
indriya5bhyah parā hy arthā artha5bhyaś ca param manas1 / manasas tu parā buddhir buddhi5 ātmā mahān parah (Kathū3.10)
mahatah param avyaktam avyaktāt purusah parah / purusāt^na param kimcit sā kāsthā sā parā gatih (Kathū3.11)
esa sarva7su bhūta7su gūdhas'ātmā na prakāśate[pra\kāś] / \dr̥śyate tv agryayā buddhi.ā sūksmayā sūksmaḍarśibhih (Kathū3.12)
yacched[\yam] vācṃanasī prāajnas tat^yacchet[\yam] jnāna ātmani / jnānam ātmani mahati niyacchet[ni\yam] tad yacchet[\yam]^śānta ātmani (Kathū3.13)
uttisthata[ut\sthā] jāgratam[\jāgr̥] prāpya[pra\āp] varān nibodhata[ni\budh] / ksurasya dhārā niśitā duratyayā durgam pathas tat kavi1p \vadanti (Kathū3.14)
aśabdam asparśam arūpam avyayam tathā^arasam nityam agandhavat^ca yat / anādi^anantam mahatah param dhruvam nicāyya[ni\ci] tam mr̥tyuṃukhāt pramucyate[pra\muc] (Kathū3.15)
nāciketam upākhyānam mr̥tyu.proktam sanātanam / uktvā[\vac] \śrutvā ca medhāvī brahma.loka7 \mahīyate (Kathū3.16)
ya imam paramam guhyam śrāvayet[\śru] brahmaṣamsadi / prayatah śrāddha.kāla7 vā tadā^ānantyāya \kalpate tadā^ānantyāya kalpata iti (Kathū3.17)

parānci khāni vyatr̥nat[vi\tr̥d] svayambhūs tasmāt parān[parānc] \paśyati na^antar.ātman / kaścid dhīrah pratyak.ātmānam aiksad[\īks] āvr̥tta.caksus^amr̥tatvam icchan[\is1] (Kathū4.1)
parācah[parānc] kāmān anuyanti[anu\i] bālas te mr̥tyu6 yanti[\i] vitatasya pāśam / atha dhīrā amr̥tatvam \viditvā dhruvam adhruva7sv iha na prārthayante[pra\arth] (Kathū4.2)
yena rūpam rasam gandham śabdān sparśāmś ca maithunān / etena^eva vijānāti[vi\jnā] kim atra pariśisyate[pari\śis] / etad vai tat (Kathū4.3)
svapna.antam jāgarita.antam ca^ubhau yena^anupaśyati[anu\pas] / mahāntam[mahat] vibhum ātmānam matvā[\man] dhīras^na śocati[\śuc] (Kathū4.4)
ya imam madhu.adam veda[\vid] ātmānam jīvam antikāt / īśānam bhūta.bhavyasya na tatas^vijugupsate[vi\gup] / etad vai tat (Kathū4.5)
yah pūrvam tapaso jātam ap.bhyah pūrvam ajāyata[\jan] / guhām praviśya[pra\viś] tisthantam[\sthā] yas^bhūta3bhir vyapaśyata[vi\paś] / etad vai tat (Kathū4.6)
yā prāna3na sambhavaty[sam\bhū] aditir devatāmayī / guhām praviśya[pra\viś] tisthantīm[\sthā] yā bhūta3bhir vyajāyata[vi\jan] / etad vai tat (Kathū4.7)
arani.or nihitas^jātavedas1 garbha iva subhr̥tas^garbhinībhih / diva7 diva īdyas^jāgr̥vadbhir havismadbhir manusya3bhir agnih / etad vai tat (Kathū4.8)
yataś ca^udeti[ut\i] sūryas^astam yatra ca gacchati[\gam] / tam devāh sarva1d'arpitās tad u na^atyeti[ati\i] kaścana / etad vai tat (Kathū4.9)
yad eva^iha tad amutra yad amutra tad anu^iha / mr̥tyu5 sa mr̥tyum \āpnoti ya iha nānā^iva \paśyati (Kathū4.10)
manasā^eva^idam āptavyam na^iha nānā^\asti kimcana / mr̥tyu5 sa mr̥tyum gacchati[\gam] ya iha nānā^iva \paśyati (Kathū4.11) [atm]
angusthaṃātrah purusas^madhya ātmani tisthati[\sthā] / īśānam bhūta.bhavyasya na tatas^vijugupsate[vi\gup] / etad vai tat (Kathū4.12)
angusthaṃātrah purusas^jyotis^iva^adhūmakah / īśānas^bhūta.bhavyasya sa eva^adya sa u śvas. / etad vai tat (Kathū4.13)
yathā^udakam durga7 vr̥stam parvata7su vidhāvati[vi\dhāv] / evam dharmān pr̥thak.paśyams[\paś] tān eva^anuvidhāvati[anuvi\dhāv] (Kathū4.14)
yathā^udakam śuddha7 śuddham āsiktam tādr̥ś^eva bhavati[\bhū] / evam muni6 vijānata[vi\jnā] ātmā bhavati[\bhū] gautama (Kathū4.15) [atm]

puram ekādaśaḍvāram ajasya^avakra.cetasah / anusthāya[anu\sthā] na śocati[\śuc] vimuktaś ca vimucyate[vi\muc] / etad vai tat (Kathū5.1)
hamsah śuciṣad[śuciṣad] vasur antariksaṣad^hotr̥1 vediṣad atithir duronaṣad. / nr̥ṣad varaṣad r̥taṣad vyomaṣad abjā gojā r̥tajā adrijā r̥tam br̥hat (Kathū5.2)
ūrdhvam prānam unnayaty[ut\nī] apānam pratyak^asyati[\as] / madhya7 vāmanam āsīnam[\as] viśva1p devā upāsate[\upa\ās] (Kathū5.3)
asya visramsamānasya[vi\srams] śarīraṣthasya dehinah / dehād vimucyamānasya kim atra pariśisyate[pari\śis] / etad vai tat (Kathū5.4)
na prāna3na na^apāna3na martyas^\jīvati kaścana / itara3na tu \jīvanti yasminn etāv upāśritau (Kathū5.5)
hanta ta idam pravaksyāmi[pra\vac] guhyam brahma sanātanam / yathā ca maranam prāpya[pra\āp] ātmā bhavati[\bhū] gautama (Kathū5.6)
yonim anya1p prapadyante[pra\pad] śarīratvāya dehinah / sthānum anya1p'anusamanti[anusam\i] yathā.karma yathā.śrutam (Kathū5.7)
ya yesu (esu?) supta7su jāgarti[\jāgr̥] kāmam kāmam purusa^nirmimānah[nis\mā] / tad eva śukram tad brahma tad eva^amr̥tam ucyate[\vac] (Kathū5.8a)
tasmiml lokāh śritāh sarva1p tad u na^atyeti[ati\i] kaścana / etad vai tat (Kathū5.8b)
agnir yathā^ekas^bhuvanam pravistas^rūpam rūpam pratir̥ūpas^babhūva[\bhū] / ekas tathā sarva.bhūta.antar.ātmā rūpam rūpam pratir̥ūpas^bahiś ca (Kathū5.9)
vāyur yathā^ekas^bhuvanam pravistas^rūpam rūpam pratir̥ūpas^babhūva[\bhū] / ekas tathā sarva.bhūta.antar.ātmā rūpam rūpam pratir̥ūpas^bahiś ca (Kathū5.10)
sūryas^yathā sarva.lokasya caksus^na \lipyate cāksusair bāhyaḍosaih / ekas tathā sarva.bhūta.antar.ātmā na \lipyate lokaḍuhkha3na bāhyah (Kathū5.11)
ekas^vaśin1 sarva.bhūta.antar.ātmā ekam rūpam bahudhā yah karoti[\kr̥] / tam ātmastham ye'anupaśyanti[anu\paś] dhīrās tesām sukham śāśvatam na^itaresām (Kathū5.12)
nityas^anityānām cetanaś cetanānām ekas^bahūnām yas^vidadhāti[vi\dhā] kāmān / tam ātmastham ye'anupaśyanti[ani\paś] dhīrās tesām śāntih śāśvatī na^itaresām (Kathū5.13)
tad etad iti manyante'anirdeśyam paramam sukham / katham nu tad vijānīyām[vi\jnā] kim u \bhāti vibhāti[vi\bhā] vā (Kathū5.14)
na tatra sūryas^\bhāti na candraṭārakam na^imā vidyutas^\bhānti kutas'ayam agnih / tam eva bhāntam anubhāti[anu\bhā] sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti[vi\bhā] (Kathū5.15)

ūrdhvaṃūlas'avāc.śākha[avānc] eso^aśvatthah sanātanah / tad eva śukram tad brahma tad eva^amr̥tam^ucyate[\vac] / (Kathū6.1a)
tasmiml lokāh śritāh sarva1p tad u na^atyeti[ati\i] kaścana / etad vai ta (Kathū6.1b)
yad idam kimca jagat sarvam prāna ejati[\ej] nihsr̥tam / mahad bhayam vajram udyatam ya etad vidur[\vid] amr̥tās te bhavanti[\bhū] (Kathū6.2)
bhayād asya^agnir \tapati bhayāt \tapati sūryah / bhayād indraś ca vāyuś ca mr̥tyur \dhāvati pancamah (Kathū6.3)
iha ced aśakad[\śak] boddhum[\budh] prāk(prānc)^śarīrasya visrasas / tatah sarga7su loka7su śarīratvāya \kalpate (Kathū6.4)
yathā^ādarśa7 tathā^ātmani(body Keith) yathā svapna7 tathā pitr̥.loka7 / yathā^apsu parīva dadr̥śe[\dr̥ś] tathā gandharva.loka7 chāyāṭapayor iva brahma.loka7 (Kathū6.5) [atm]
indriyānām pr̥thak.bhāvam udaya.astamāu ca tat / pr̥thak.utpadyamānānām matvā[\man] dhīras^na śocati[\śuc] (Kathū6.6)
indriya5bhyah param manas^manasah sattvam uttamam / sattvād adhi mahān ātmā mahatas'avyaktam uttamam (Kathū6.7)
avyaktāt tu parah purusas^vyāpakas^alinga eva ca / yam jnātvā \mucyate jantur amr̥tatvam ca gacchati[\gam] (Kathū6.8)
na samdr̥śe tisthati[\sthā] rūpam asya na caksusā \paśyati kaścana^enam / hr̥dā manīsā manasā^abhiklr̥ptas[abhi\klr̥p]^ya etad vidur[\vid] amr̥tās te bhavanti[\bhū] (Kathū6.9)
yadā panca^avatisthante[ava\sthā] jnānāni manasā saha / buddhiś ca na viceestati[vi\cest] tām āhuh[\ah] paramām gatim (Kathū6.10)
tām yogam iti \manyante sthirām indriyaḍhāranām / apramattas tadā bhavati[\bhū] yogas^hi prabhava.apyayau (Kathū6.11)
na^eva vācā na manasā prāptum[pra\āp] śakyas^na caksusā / asti[\as]^iti bruvatas[\brū]'anyatra katham tad upalabhyate[upa\labh] (Kathū6.12)
asti[\as]^ity eva^upalabdhavyas tattva.bhāva3na ca^ubhayoh / asti[\as]^ity eva^upalabdhasya tattva.bhāvah prasīdati[pra\sad] (Kathū6.13)
yadā sarva1p pramucyante[pra\muc] kāmā ye'asya hr̥di \śritāh / atha martyas^amr̥tas^bhavaty[\bhū] atra brahma samaśnute[sam\aś] (Kathū6.14)
yadā sarva1p prabhidyante[pra\bhid] hr̥dayasya^iha granthi1p / atha marthas'amr̥tas^bhavaty[\bhū] etāvad^hy anuśāsanam (Kathū6.15)
śatam ca^ekā ca hr̥dayasya nādī1p tāsām mūrdhānam abhinihsr̥tā[abhinis\sr̥]^ekā / tayā^ūrdhvam āyann[ā\i] amr̥tatvam eti[\i] visvan[visvanc]^anyā utkramana7 bhavanti[\bhū] (Kathū6.16)
angusthaṃātrah puruso^antar.ātmā sadā janānām hr̥daya7 samnivistah / (Kathū6.17a)
tam svāt^śarīrāt pravr̥het[pra\vr̥h]^munjād iva^isīkām dhairya3na / tam vidyāt[\vid]^śukram amr̥tam tam vidyāt[\vid]^śukram amr̥tam iti (Kathū6.17)
mr̥tyu.proktām naciketas^atha labdhvā[\labh] vidyām etām yoga.vidhim ca kr̥tsnam / brahma prāptas^virajas^abhūd[\bhū] vimr̥tyur anyas^apy evam yas^vid[\vid?] adhyātmam eva (Kathū6.18)
saha nāv \avatu / saha nau bhunaktu[\bhuj] / saha vīryam karavāvahai[\kr̥] / tejasvi na^avadhītam \astu mā vidvisāvahia[\dvis] (Kathū6.19) =End of Kathū=

<Kena ūpanisad>(Kenaū)
om kena^isitam \patati presitam[pra\is] manas^kena prānah prathamah praiti[pra\i] yuktah / kena^isitām[\is] vācam imām \vadanti caksus^śrotram ka u devas^yunakti[\yuj] (Kenaū1.1)
śrotrasya śrotram manaso manas^yad vācas^ha vācam sa u prānasya prānah / caksusaś caksus^atimucya[ati\muc] dhīrāh pretya[pra\i]^asmāl lokād amr̥tā bhavanti[\bhū] (Kenaū1.2)
na tatra caksus^gacchati[\gam] na vāc^gacchati[\gam] na^u manas. / na vidmas[\vid]^na vijānīmas[vi\jnā]^yathā^etad anuśisyāt[anu\śis] (Kenaū1.3)
anyad eva tad viditād[\vid] atho aviditād adhi / iti śuśruma[\śru] pūrva6sām ye nas tad vyācacaksire[vyā\caks] (Kenaū1.4)
yad vācā^anabhyuditam[abhi\vad] yena vāc^abhyudyate[abhi\vad] / tad eva brahma tvam \viddhi na^idam yad imam upāsate[upa\ās] (Kenaū1.5)
yan manasā na \manute yena^āhur[\ah] manas^matam / tad eva brahma tvam \viddhi na^idam yad idam upāsate[upa\ās] (Kenaū1.6)
yat^caksusā na \paśyati yena caksus2p \paśyati / tad eva brahma tvam viddhi na^idam yad idam upāsate[upa\ās] (Kenaū1.7)
yat^śrotra3na na śr̥noti[\śru] yena śrotram idam śrutam / tad eva brahma tvam \viddhi na^idam yad idam upāsate[upa\ās] (Kenaū1.8)
yat prāna3na na prānini[pra\an] yena prānah pranīyate[pra\nī] / tad eva brahma tvam viddhi na^idam yad idam upāsate[upa\ās] (Kenaū1.9)

yadi \manyase su veda[\vid]^iti dabhram eva^api nūnam tvam vettha[\vid] brahmanas^rūpam yad asya tvam yad asya deva7sv atha nu mīmāmsyam[\man] eva te \manye viditam[\vid] (Kenaū2.1) [atm]
na^aham \manye su veda[\vid]^iti na^u na veda[\vid]^iti veda[\vid] ca / yas^nas tad veda[\vid] tad veda[\vid] na^u na veda[\vid]^iti veda[\vid] ca (Kenaū2.2)
yasya^amatam tasya matam matam yasya na veda[\vid] sah / avijnātam vijānatām vijnātam avijānatām (Kenaū2.3)
pratibodha.viditam matam amr̥tatvam hi \vindate / ātmanā \vindate vīryam vidyayā \vindate'amr̥tam (Kenaū2.4) [atm]
iha ced avedīd[\vid] atha satyam asti na ced iha^avedīt[\vid]^mahatī vinastih / bhuta7su bhūta7su vicitya[vi\ci] dhīrāh pretya[pra\i]^asmāl lokād amr̥tā bhavanti[bhū\] (Kenaū2.5)

brahma ha deva5bhyas^vijigye[vi\ji] tasya ha brahmanas^vijaya7 devā amahīyanta[\mah] / ta aiksanta[\īks]^asmākam eva^ayam vijayas^asmākam eva^ayam mahimā^iti (Kenaū3.1)
tad dha^esām vijajnau[vi\jnā] tebhyas^ha prādur.babhūva[prādur\bhū] tan na vyajānata[vi\jnā] kim idam yaksam iti (Kenaū3.2)
te'agnim abruvan[\brū]^jātaveda etad vijānīhi[vi\jnā] kim etad yaksam iti tathā^iti (Kenaū3.3)
tad abhyadravat[abhi\dru] tam abhyavadat[abhi\vad] kas'asi[\as]^ity agnir vā aham \asmi^ity abravīt[\brū]^jātavedas1 vā aham \asmi^iti (Kenaū3.4)
tasmims tvayi kim vīryam ity api^idam sarvam daheyam[\dah] yad idam pr̥thivi.ām iti (Kenaū3.5)
tasmai tr̥nam nidadhāv[ni\dhā] etad daha[\dah]^iti tad upapreyāya[upapra\i] sarvajava3na tan na śaśāka[\śak] dagdhum[\dah] sa tata eva nivavr̥te[ni\vr̥t] na^etad aśakam[\śak] vijnātum[vi\jnā] yad etad yaksam iti (Kenaū3.6)
atha vāym abruvan[\brū] vāyu8 etad vijānīhi[vi\jnā] kim etad yaksam iti tathā^iti (Kenaū3.7)
tad abhyadravat[abhi\dru] tam abhyavadat[abhi\vad] kas'\asi^iti vāyur vā aham \asmi^ity abravīt[\brū]^mātariśvan1 vā aham \asmi^iti (Kenaū3.8)
tasmins tvayi kim vīryam ity api^idam sarvam ādadīya[ā\dā] yad idam pr̥thivi.ām iti (Kenaū3.9)
tasmai tr̥nam nidadhāv[ni\dhā] etad ādatsva[ā\dā]^iti tad upapreyāya[upapra\i] sarvajava3na tan an śaśāka[\śak]^ādātum[ā\dā] sa tata eva nivavr̥te[ni\vr̥t] na^etad aśakam[\śak] vijnātum[vi\jnā] yad etad yaksam iti (Kenaū3.10)
atha^indram abruvan[\brū] maghavat8^etad vijānīhi[vi\jnā] kim etad yaksam iti tathā^iti tad abhyadravat[abhi\dru] tasmāt tirodadhe[tiras\dhā](Kenaū3.11)
sa tasminn eva^ākāśa7 striyam ājagāma[ā\gam] bahu.śobhamānām umām haimavatīm tām ha^uvāca[\vac] kim etad yaksam iti (Kenaū3.12)

sā brahma^iti ha^uvāca[\vac] brahmano vā etad vijaya7 \mahīyadhvam iti tato ha^eva vidām.cakāra[\vid] brahma^iti (Kenaū4.1)
tasmād vā ete devā atitarām iva^anyān devān yad agnir vāyur indras te hy enan nedistam pasparśus[\spr̥ś] te hy enat prathamas^vidām.cakāra[\vid] brahma^iti (Kenaū4.2)
tasmād vā indras'atitarām iva^anyān devān sa hy enat^nedistham pasparśa[\spr̥ś] sa hy enat prathamas^vidām.cakāra brahma^iti (Kenaū4.3)
tasya^esa ādeśas^yad etad vidyutas^vyadyutad[\vi\dyut] ā iti^it^nyamīmisad[ni\mis] ā ity adhidaivatam (Kenaū4.4)
atha^adhyātmam yad etad gacchati[\gam]^iva ca manas'anena ca^etad upasmaraty[upa\smr̥] abhīksnam samkalpah (Kenaū4.5)
tadd ha tat.vanam[tadvana] nāma tadvanam ity upāsitavyam[upa\ās] sa ya etad evam veda[\vid]^abhi ha^enam sarvāni bhūtāni samvāmchanti[abhisam\vānch] (Kenaū4.6)
upanisadam bho \brūhi^ity uktā ta upanisad brāhmīm vāva ta upanisadam abrūma[\brū]^iti (Kenaū4.7)
tasmai tapas^damah karma^iti pratisthā vedāh sarvaṇgāni satyam āyatanam (Kenaū4.8)
yo vā etām evam veda[\vid]^apahatya[apa\han] pāpmānam ananta7 svarga7 loka7 jyeya7 pratitisthati[prati\sthā] pratitisthati (Kenaū4.9) =End of Kenaū=


<Chāngodya ūpanisad>(Chū)
om / āpyāyantu[ā\pyai] mama^angāni vāc^prānaś caksus^śrotram atha^u balam indriyāni ca sarvāni sarvam brahma.upanisadam - (Chū.introd)
mā^aham brahma nirākuryām[nirā\kr̥] mā mā brahma nirākarod[nisā\kr̥] anirākaranam \astv anirākaranam \astu - (Chū.introd)
tā^ātmani nirata7 ya upanisadṣu dharmās te mayi santu[\as] te mayi santu[\as] // om śāntih śāntih śāntih. (Chū.introd)

om ity etad aksaram udgītham upāsīta[upa\ās] / om iti hy udgāyati[ut\gai] tasya^upavyākhyānam (Chū1.1.1)
esām bhūtānām pr̥thivī rasah pr̥thivi.ā āpas^rasah / apām osadhi1p rasa osadhīnām purusas^rasah purusasya vāc^rasas^vāca r̥c^rasa r̥cah sāma rasah sāmna[sāman] udgīthas^rasah (Chū1.1.2)
sa esa rasānām rasatamah pramah para.ardhyas^astamas^yad udgīthah (Chū1.1.3)
katamā katamā^r̥c^katamat katamat sāma katamah katama udgītha iti vimr̥stam bhavati (Chū1.1.4)
vāc^eva^r̥c^prānah sāma^om ity etad aksaram udgītah / tad vā etat^mithunam yad vāc^ca prānaś ca^r̥c^ca sāma ca (Chū1.1.5)
tad etat^mithunam om ity etasminn aksara7 samsr̥jyate[sam\sr̥j] yadā vai mithunau samāgacchata[samā\gam] āpayatas[\āp] vai tāv anyonyasya kāmam (Chū1.1.6)
āpayitr̥1 ha vai kāmānām bhavati ya etad evam vidvat1m aksaram udgītham upāste[upa\ās] (Chū1.1.7)
tad vā etad anujnā^aksaram yad dhi kimca^anujanāty[anu\jnā] om ity eva tad^āha^esa eva samr̥ddhir yad anujnā samardhayitr̥1 ha vai kāmānām bhavati ya etad evam vidvat1m aksaram udgītham upāste[upa\ās] (Chū1.1.8)
tena^iyam trayī vidyā vartate[\vr̥t] om ity āśrāvayaty[ā\śru] om iti śamsaty[\śams] om ity udgāyati[ut\gai] etasya^eva^aksarasya^apaciti.ai mahiman3 rasa3na (Chū1.1.9)
tena^ubhau kurutas[\kr̥]^yaś ca^etad evam veda[\vid] yaś ca na veda[\vid] (Chū1.1.10a)
nānā tu vidyā ca^avidyā ca yad eva vidyayā karoti[\kr̥] śraddhayā^upanisadā tad eva vīryavattaram bhavati^iti khalsv etasya^eva^aksarasya^upavyākhyānam bhavati (Chū1.1.10b)

deva.asurā ha vai yatra samyetira[sam\yat] ubhaye prājāpatyās tad dha devā udgītham ājahrur[ā\hr̥] anena^enān abhibhavisyāma[abhi\bhū] iti (Chū1.2.1)
te ha nāsikyam prānam udgītham upāsāmcakrire[upa\ās] tam ha^asurāh pāpnamā vividhus[\vyadh] tasmāt tena^ubhayam jighrati[\ghrā] surabhi ca durgandhi ca pāpmanā hy esa viddhah[\vyadh] (Chū1.2.2)
atha ha vācam udgītham upāsāmcakrire[upa\ās] tā ha^asurāh pāpmanā vividhu[\vyadh] tasmāt tayā^ubhayam vadati[\vad] satyam ca^anr̥tam ca pāpmanā hy esā viddhā[\vyadh] (Chū1.2.3)
atha ha caksus^udgītham upāsāmcakrire[upa\ās] tad dha^asurāh pāpmanā vividhu[\vyadh] tasmāt tena^ubhayam \paśyati darśanīyam ca^adarśanīyam ca pāpmanā hy etad viddham[\vyadh] (Chū1.2.4)
atha ha śrotram udgītham upāsāmcakrire[upa\ās] tad dha^asurāh pāpmanā vividhus[\vyadh] tasmāt tena^ubhayam śr̥noti[\śru] śravanīyam ca^aśravanīyamca pāpmanā hy etad viddham[\vyadh] (Chū1.2.5)
atha ha manas^udgītham upāsāmcakrire[upa\ās] tad dha^asurāh pāpmanā vividhus[\vyadh] tasmāt tena^ubhayam samkalpate[sam\kalp] samkalpanīyam ca^asamkalpanīyam ca pāpmanā hy etad viddham[\vyadh] (Chū1.2.6)
atha ha ya eva^ayam mukhyah prānas tam udgītham upāsāmcakrire[upa\ās] tam ha^asurā \r̥tvā vidadhvamsur[vi\dhvams] yathā^aśmānam ākhanam \r̥tvā vidhvamseta[vi\dhvams]^evam (Chū1.2.7)
yathā^aśmānam ākhanam \r̥tvā vidhvamsata[vi\dhvams] evam ha^eva sa vidhvamsate[vi\dhvams] ya evam.vidi pāpam \kāmayate yaś ca^enam abhidāsati[abhi\das/abhi\dās] sa eso^aśmā^ākhanah (Chū1.2.8)
na^eva^etena surabhi na durgandhi vijānāty[vi\jnā] apahata.pāpmā hy esa tena yad \aśnāti yat pibati[\pā] tena^itarān prānān \avati (Chū1.2.9a)
etam u eva^antatas'avittvā[\vind]^utkrāmati[ut\kram] vyādadāty[vyā\dā] eva^antata iti (Chū1.2.9)
tam ha^angiras1 udgītham upāsāmcakra[upa\ās] etam u eva^angirasam manyante[\man]'angānām yad rasah (Chū1.2.10)
tena tam ha br̥haspatir udgītham upāsāmcakra[upa\ās] etam u eva br̥haspatim \manyante vāc^hi br̥hatī tasyā esa patih (Chū1.2.11)
tena tam ha^ayāsya udgītham upāsāmcakra[upa\ās] etam u eva^ayāsyam manyanta[\man] āsyād yad ayate[\i] (Chū1.2.12)
tena tam ha balas^dālbhyas^vidām.cakāra[\vid] / sa ha naimiśīyānām udgātr̥1 babhūva[\bhū] sa ha sma^ebhyah kāmān āgāyati[ā\gai] (Chū1.2.13)
āgātr̥1 ha vai kāmānām bhavati ya etad evam vidvat1m aksaram udgītham upāsta[upa\ās] ity adhyātmam (Chū1.2.14)

atha^adhidaivatam ya eva^asau \tapati tam udgītham upāsīta[upa\ās]^udyan[ut\i] vā esa prajābhya udgāyati[ut\gai] / udyams[ut\i] tamas^bhayam apahanty[apa\han] apahantr̥1 ha vai bhayasya tamaso bhavati ya evam veda[\vid] (Chū1.3.1)
samāna u eva^ayam ca^asau ca^usnas'ayam usnas'asau svara iti^imam ācaksate[ā\caks] svara iti pratyāsvara ity amum tasmād vā etam imam amum ca^udgītham upāsīta[upa\ās] (Chū1.3.2)
atha khalu vyānam eva^udgītham upāsīta[upa\ās] yad vai prāniti[pra\an] sa prānas^yad apānini[apa\an] so^apānah (Chū1.3.3a)
tha yah prāna.apānayoh samdhih sa vyānas^yas^vyānah sā vāc1 / tasmād aprānann[pra\an] anapānan[apa\an] vācam abhivyāharati[abhivyā\hr̥] (Chū1.3.3b)
yā vāc^sā^r̥c^asmād aprānan[pra\an] anapānann[apa\an] r̥cam abhivyāharati[abhivyā\hr̥] yā^r̥c^tat sāma tasmād aprānann[pra\an] anapānan[apa\an] sāma gāyati[\gai] yat sāma sa udgīthas tasmād aprānann[pra\an] apānann[apa\an] udgāyati[ut\gai] (Chū1.3.4)
atas^yāny anyāni vīryavanti karmāni yathā^agni6 mathanam āji6 saranam dr̥dhasya dhanusa āyamanam aprānann[pra\an] anapānams[apa\an] tāni karoty[\kr̥] etasya hetu6 vyānam eva^udgītham upāsīta[upa\ās] (Chū1.3.5)
atha khalu^udgītha.aksarāny upāsīta[upa\ās]^ut^gī^tha iti prāna eva^ut prāna3na hy uttisthati[ut\sthā] vāc^gīr vācas^ha gira ity ācaksate[ā\caks]'annam tham anna7 hi^idam sarvam sthitam (Chū1.3.6)
dyaur eva^ut^antariksam gīh pr̥thivī tham āditya eva^ut^vāyur gīr agnis tham sāma.veda eva^ut yajurvedas^gīr r̥gvedas tham dugdha[\duh]'asmai vāc^doham yo vācas^dohas'annavān anna.adas^bhavati ya etāny evam vidvat1m udgītha.aksarāny upāsta[upa\ās] udgītha iti (Chū1.3.7)
atha khalu^āsisṣamr̥ddhir upasaranāni^ity upāsīta[upa\ās] yena sāman3 stosyan[\stu] syāt[\as] sāma^upadhāvet[upa\dhāv] (Chū1.3.8)
yasyām r̥c tām r̥cam yad ārseyam tam r̥sim yām devatām abhistosyan[abhi\stu] syāt[\as] tām devatām upadhāvet[upa\dhāv] (Chū1.3.9)
yena chandasā stosyan[\stu] syāt[\as] tat^chandas^upadhāved[upa\dhāv] yena stoma3na stosyamānah[\stu] syāt[\as] tam stomam upadhāvet[upa\dhāv] (Chū1.3.10)
yām diśam abhistosyan[abhi\stu] syāt[\as] tām diśam upadhāvet[upa\dhāv] (Chū1.3.11)
ātmānam antata upasr̥tya[upa\sr̥] stuvīta[\stu] kāmam dhyāyann[\dhyā] apramattas'abhyāśas^ha yad asmai sa kāmah samr̥dhyeta[sam\r̥dh] yat.kāmah stuvīta[\stu]^iti yat.kāmah stuvīta[\stu]^iti (Chū1.3.12)

om ity etad aksaram udgītham upāsīta[upa\ās]^om ity hy udgāyati[ut\gai] tasya^upavyākhyānam (Chū1.4.1)
devā vai mr̥tyu5 bibhyatas[\bhī] trayīm vidyām prāviśams[pra\viś] te chandas.bhir acchādayan[\chad] yad ebhir acchādayams[\chad] tat^chandasām chandastvam (Chū1.4.2)
tān u tatra mr̥tyur yathā matsyam udaka7 paripaśyed[pari\paś] evam paryapaśyad[pari\paś] r̥ci sāman7 yajusi (Chū1.4.3a)
te nu viditvā[\vid]^ūrdhvā r̥cah sāman5 yajusah svaram eva prāviśan[pra\viś] (Chū1.4.3b)
yadā vā r̥cam āpnoty[\āp] om ity eva^atisvaraty[ati\svar] evam sāma^evam yajur esa u svaras^yad etad aksaram etad amr̥tam abhayam tat praviśya[pra\viś] devā amr̥tā abhayā abhavan[\bhū] (Chū1.4.4)
sa ya etad evam vidvat1m aksaram pranauty[pra\nu] etad eva^aksaram svaram amr̥tam abhayam praviśati[pra\viś] tat praviśya[pra\viś] yad amr̥tā devās tad amr̥tas^bhavati (Chū1.4.5)

atha khalu ya udgīthah sa pranavas yah pranavah sa udgītha ity asau vā āditya udgītha esa pranava om iti hy esa svarann[\svar] eti[\i] (Chū1.5.1)
etam u eva^aham abhyāgāsisam[abhi\gai] tasmāt^mama tvam ekas'asi^iti ha kausītakih putram uvāca[\vac] rasmīms tvam paryāvartayād[paryā\vr̥t] bahu1p vai te bhavisyanti[\bhū]^ity adhidaivatam (Chū1.5.2)
atha^adhyātmam ya eva^ayam mukhyah prānas tam udgītham upāsīta[upa\ās] om iti hy esa svarann[\svar] eti[\i] (Chū1.5.3)
etam u eva^aham abhyagāsisam[abhi\gai] tasmāt^mama tvam ekas^asi^iti ha kausītakih putram uvāca[\vac] prānāms tvam bhūman2 abhigāyatād[abhi\gai] bahu1p vai me bhavisyanti^iti (Chū1.5.4)

iyam eva^r̥c^agnih sāma tad etad etasyām r̥ci^adhyūdham[adhi\vah] sāma tasmād r̥ci^adhyūdham[adhi\vah] sāma gīyata[\gai] iyam eva sā^agnir amas tat sāma (Chū1.6.1)
antariksam eva^r̥c^vāyuh sāma tad etad etasyām r̥ci^adhyūdham[abhi\vah] sāma tasmād r̥ci^adhyūdham[abhi\vah] sāma gīyate[\gai]'antariksam eva sā vāyur amas tat sāma (Chū1.6.2)
dyaur eva^r̥c^ādityah sāma tad etad etasyām r̥ci^adhyūdham[adhi\vah] sāma tasmād r̥ci^adhyūdham[adhi\vah] sāma gīyate[\gai] dyaur eva sā^ādityas^amas tat sāma (Chū1.6.3)
naksatrāny eva^r̥c^candramas1 sāma tad etad etasyām r̥cy adhyūdham[adhi\vah] sāma tasmād r̥cy adhyūdham sāma gīyate[\gai] naksatrāny eva sā candramas1^amas tat sāma (Chū1.6.4)
atha yad eva^etad ādityasya śuklam bhāh sā^eva^r̥c^atha yan nīlam parah kr̥snam tat sāma tad etad etasyām r̥cy adhyūdham[adhi\vah] sāma tasmād r̥cy adhyūdham[adhi\vah] sāma gīyate[\gai] (Chū1.6.5)

atha yad etad aksi6 śuklam bhāh sā^eva^r̥c^atha yan nīlam parah kr̥snam tat sāma tad etad etasyām r̥cy adhyūdham[adhi\vah] sāma tasmād r̥cy adhyūdham[adhi\vah] sāma gīyate[\gai] / atha yad eva^etad aksi6 śuklam bhāh sā^eva sā^atha yan nīlam parah kr̥snam tad amas tat sāma (Chū1.7.4)

kā sāman6 gatir iti svara iti ha^uvāca[\vac] svarasya kā gatir iti prāna iti ha^uvāca[\vac] prānasya kā gatir atyannnam iti ha^uvāca[\vac]^annasya kā gatir ity āpa iti ha^uvāca[\vac] (Chū1.8.4)

loka7su panca.vidham sāma^upāsīta[upa\ās] pr̥thivī him.kārah / agnih prastāvas'antariksam udgītha ādityah pratihāras^dyaur nidhanam ity ūrdhva7su (Chū2.2.1)

prāna7su panca.vidham parovarīyas^sāma^upāsīta[upa\ās] prānas^him.kāras^vāc^prastāvaś caksus^udgīthah śrotram pratihāras^manas^nidhanam parovarīyas1np vā etāni (Chū2.7.1)
parovarīyas^ha^asya bhavati parovarīyasas^ha lokān jayati[\ji] ya etad evam vidvat1m prāna7su panca.vidham parovarīyas^sāma^upāsta[upa\ās] iti tu panca.vidhasya (Chū2.7.2)

atha sapta.vidhasya vāci sapta.vidham sāma^upāsīta[upa\ās] yat kimca vācas^hum iti sa him.kāras^yat pra^iti sa prastāvas yad ā^iti sa ādih (Chū2.8.1)

dugdhe[\duh]'asmai vāc^doham yo vācas^dohas'annavān anna.adas^bhavati ya etad evam vidvat1m vāci sapta.vidham sāma^upāste[upa\ās] (Chū2.8.3)

atha khalu^amum ādityam sapta.vidham sāma^upāsīta[upa\ās] sarvadā samas tena sāma mām prati mām prati^iti sarva3na samas tena sāma (Chū2.9.1)
tasminn imāni sarvāni bhūtāny anvāyattāni^iti vidyāt[\vid] tasya yat purodayāt sa him.kāras tad asya paśu1p'anvāyattās tasmāt te him kurvanti[\kr̥] him.kāra.bhājinas^hy etasya sāman6 (Chū2.9.2)
atha yat prathama.udita7 sa prastāvas tad asya manusyā anvāyattās tasmāt te prastuti.kāmāh praśamsā.kāmāh prastāva.bhājinas^hy etasya sāman6 (Chū2.9.3)
atha yat samgava.velāyām sa ādis tad asya vayāmsy[vayas] anvāyattāni tasmāt tāny antariksa7'anārambanāny ādāya[ā\dā]^ātmānam paripatanty[pari\pat] ādi.bhājīni hy etasya sāman6 (Chū2.9.4)

atha yad ūrdhvam madhyandināt prāk[prānc]^apara.ahnāt sa pratihāras tad asya garbhā anvāyattās tasmāt te pratihr̥tā[prati\hr̥] na^avapadyante[ava\pad] pratihāra.bhājino hy etasya sāman6 (Chū2.9.6)
atha yad ūrdhvam apara.ahnāt prāk[pranc]^astamayāt sa upadravas tad asya^aranyā anvāyattās tasmāt te purusam dr̥stvā[\dr̥ś] kaksam śvabhram ity upadravanty[upa\dru] upadrava.bhājino hy etasya sāman6 (Chū2.9.7)
atha yat prathama.astamita7 tat^nidhanam tad asya pitr̥1p'anvāyattās tasmāt tān nidadhati[ni\dhā] nidhana.bhājinas^hy etasya sāman6 evam khalu^amum ādityam sapta.vidham sāma^upāste[upa\ās] (Chū2.9.8)

ekavimsati.ā^ādityam \āpnoty ekavimśas^vā itas'asāv ādityas^dvāvimśa3na param ādityāj jayati[\ji] tat^nākam tad viśokam (Chū2.10.5)

vinardi sāman6 vr̥ne[\vr̥] paśavyam ity agni6 udgīthas'aniruktah prajāpati6 niruktah somasya mr̥du ślaksnam vāyu6 ślaksnam balavad indrasya krauncam br̥haspati6 apadhvāntam varunasya tān sarvān eva^upaseveta[upa\sev] vārunam tv eva varjayet[\vr̥j] (Chū2.22.1)

om asau vā ādityas^devaṃadhu tasya dyaur eva tiraścīna.vamśas'antariksam apūpas^marīci1p putrāh (Chū3.1.1)
tasya ye prāncas^raśmi1p tā eva^asya prācyas[prānc] madhuṇādī1p / r̥ca eva madhu.kr̥ta r̥gveda eva puspam tā amr̥tā āpas tā va etā r̥cah (Chū3.1.2)
etam r̥gvedam abhyatapams[abhi\tap] tasya^abhitaptasya yaśas tejas^indriyam vīryam anna.adyam rasas^ajāyata[\jan] (Chū3.1.3)

atha ye'asya daksinā raśmi1p tā eva^asya daksinā madhuṇādī1p yajus1p eva madhu.kr̥tas^yajurveda eva puspam tā amr̥tā āpas. (Chū3.2.1)

atha ye'asya pratyancas^raśmi1p tā eva^asya pratīcyas[pratyanc]^madhuṇādī1p sāmāny eva madhu.kr̥tah sāmaveda eva puspam tā amr̥tā āpas. (Chū3.3.1)

atha ye'asya^ūrdhvā raśmi1p tā eva^asya^ūrdhvā madhuṇādī1p guhyā eva^ādeśā madhu.kr̥tas^brahma^eva puspam tā amr̥tā āpas. (Chū3.5.1)

tad yat prathamam amr̥tam tad vasu1p upajīvanty[upa\jīv] agninā mukha3na na vai devā aśnanti[\aś] na pibanti[\pā]^etad eva^amr̥tam dr̥stvā[\dr̥ś] tr̥pyanti[\tr̥p] (Chū3.6.1)

sa yāvad ādityah purastād udetr̥1[ut\i] paścād astam etr̥1[\i] vasūnām eva tāvad ādhipatyam svārājyam paryetr̥1[pati\i] (Chū3.6.4)

atha yad dvitīyam amr̥tam tad rudrā upajīvanti[upa\jīv]^indra3na mukha3na na vai vedā aśnanti[\aś] na pibanty[\pā] etad eva^amr̥tam dr̥stvā[dr̥ś] tr̥pyanti (Chū3.7.1)

yathā kr̥tāya.vijitāya^adhareyāh samyanty[sam\i] evam enam sarvam tad abhisamaiti[abhisam\i] yat kimca prajāh sādhu kurvanti[\kr̥] yas tad veda[\vid] yat sa veda[\vid] sa mayā^etad ukta iti (Chū4.1.6)

so^adhastāt^śakatasya pāmānam[pāman] kasamānam[\kas] upopaviveśa[upopa\viś] tam ha^abhyuvāda[abhi\vad] tvam nu bhagavah sayugman1 raikva ity(Chū4.1.8a)
aham hy arā3 iti ha pratijajne[prati\jnā] sa ha ksattr̥1^avidam[\vid] iti pratyeyāya[prati\i] (Chū4.1.8b)

tad u ha jānaśrutih pautrāyanah sas.śatāni go6p niskam aśvatarīr̥atham tad ādāya[ā\dā] praticakrame[prati\kram] tam ha^abhyuvāda[abhi\vad] (Chū4.2.1)
raikva^imāni sas.śatāni go6p ayam niskas'ayam aśvatarīr̥athas^nu me^etām bhagavah^devatām śādhi[\śās] yām devatām upāssa[upa\ās] iti (Chū4.2.2)
tam u ha parah pratyuvāca[prati\vac]^aha ha^are tvā śūdra tava^eva saha gobhir astv[\as] iti (Chū4.2.3a)
tad u ha punar eva jānaśrutih pautrāyanah sahasram go6p niskam aśvatarīr̥atham duhitr̥2 tad ādāya[ā\dā] praticakrame[prati\kram] (Chū4.2.3b)
tam ha^abhyuvāda[abhi\vad] raikva^idam sahasram go6p ayam niskas'ayam aśvatarīr̥atha iyam jāyā^ayam grāmas^yasminn āsse[\ās] anv eva mā bhagavah śādhi[anu\śās]^iti (Chū4.2.4)
tasyā ha mukham upodgr̥hnan[upot\grah] uvāca[\vac]^ājahāra[ā\hr̥]^imāh śūdra^anena^eva mukha3na^ālāpayisyathā[ā\lap] iti (Chū4.2.5a)
te ha^ete raikvaparnā nāma mahā.vr̥sa7su yatra^asmā uvāsa[\vas] tasmai ha^uvāca[\vac] (Chū4.2.5b)

vāyur vāva samvargas^yadā vā agnir udvāyati[ut\vā] vāyum eva^apyeti[api\i] yadā sūryas^astam eti[\i] vāyum eva^apyeti[api\i] yadā candras'astam eti[\i] vāyum eva^apyeti[api\i] (Chū4.3.1)
yad āpa ucchusyante[ut\śus] vāyum eva^apiyanti[api\i] vāyur hy eva^etān sarvān samvr̥nkta[sam\vr̥j] ity adhidaivatam (Chū4.3.2)
atha^adhyātmam prānas^vāva samvargah sa yadā svapiti[\svap] prānam eva vāc^apyeti[api\i] prānam caksus^prānam śrotram prānam manas^prānas hy eva^etān sarvān samvr̥nkta[sam\vr̥j] iti (Chū4.3.3)
tau vā etau dvau samvargau vāyur eva deva7su prānah prāna7su (Chū4.3.4) [atm]
atha ha śaunakam ca kāpeyam abhipratārinam ca kāksasenim parivisyamānau[pari\vis] brahmacārin1 bibhikse[\bhiks] tasmā u ha na dadatuh[\dā] (Chū4.3.5)
sa ha^uvāca mahā.ātmanaś caturas^deva ekah kah sa jagāra[\gr̥r̥] bhuvanasya gopās tam kāpeya na^abhipaśyanti[abhi\paś] martyā abhipratārin bahudhā vasantam[\vas] yasmai vā etad annam tasmā etat^na dattam[\dā] iti (Chū4.3.6)
tad u ha śainakah kāpeyah pratimanvānah[prati\man] pratyeyāya[prati\i]^ātmā devānām janitr̥1 prajānām hiranyaḍamstras^babhasas[bhaksana.śīla Z]'anasūrir mahāntam asya mahiman2 āhur[\ah] anadyamānas^yad anannam atti[\ad]^(Chū4.3.7a)

satyakāmas^ha jābālas^jabālām mātr̥2 āmantrayām.cakre[ā\mantr] brahmacaryam bhavati vivatsyāmi[vi\vas] kim.gotras^nu^aham asmi[\as]^iti (Chū4.4.1)
sā ha^enam uvāca[\vac] na^aham etad veda[\vid] tāta yad.gotras tvam asi bahu^aham carantī[\car] paricārinī yauvana7 tvām ālabhe[\labh] sā^aham etat^na veda[\vid] yat.gotras tvam asi (Chū4.4.2a)
jabālā tu nāma^aham asmi satyakāmas^nāma tvam asi sa satyakāma eva jābālas^bruvīthā[\brū] iti (Chū4.4.2b)
sa ha hāridrumatam gautamam etya[\i]^uvāca[\vac] brahmacaryam bhagavati vatsyāmy[\vas] upeyām[upa\i] bhagavantam iti (Chū4.4.3)
tam ha^uvāca[\vac] kim.gotras^nu somya^asi[\as]^iti sa ha^uvāca na^aham etad veda[\vid] bho yat.gotras'aham asmy[\as] apr̥ccham[\prach] mātr̥2 (Chū4.4.4a)
sā mā pratyabravīd[prati\brū] bahu^aham carantī[\car] paricārinī yauvana7 tvām alabhe[\labh] sā^aham etat^na veda[\vid] yat.gotras tvam asi(Chū4.4.4b)

tam ha^uvāca[\vac] na^etad abrāhmanas^vivaktum[vi\vac] arhati[\arh] samidham somya^āhara[ā\hr̥]^upa tvā nesye[upa\nī] na satyād agā[\gā] iti(Chū4.4.5a)
tam upanīya[upa\nī] kr̥sānām alabānām catur.śatā gā[go] nirākr̥tya[nirā\kr̥]^uvāca[\vac]^imāh somya^anusamvraja[anusam\vraj]^iti (Chū4.4.5b)
tā abhiprasthāpayan[abhipra\sthā]^uvāca[\vac] na^asahasra3na^āvarteya[ā\vr̥t]^iti sa ha varsa.ganam provāsa[pra\vas] tā yadā sahasram sampeduh[sam\pad] (Chū4.4.5c)

atha ha^enam r̥sabhas'abhyuvāda[abhi\vad] satyakāma3 iti bhagavah^iti ha pratiśuśrāva[prati\śru] prāptāh somya sahasram smah[\as] prāpaya[pra\āp] na ācārya.kulam (Chū4.5.1)

agnis te pādam vaktr̥1^iti sa ha śvas.bhūte gā abhiprasthāpayām.cakāra[abhipra\sthā] (Chū4.6.1a)

etam samyadvāma ity ācaksata[ā\caks] etam hi sarvāni vāmāny abhisamyanti[abhisam\i] sarvāny enam vāmāny abhisamyanti[abhisam\i] ya evam veda[\vid] (Chū4.15.2)

prajāpatir lokān abhyatapat[abhi\tap] tesām tapyamānānām rasān prāvr̥had[pra\vr̥h] agnim pr̥thivī5 vāyum antariksād ādityam divah[dyaus] (Chū4.17.1)

tad yad r̥cṭas^risyed[\ris] bhūr^svāhā^iti gārhapatya7 juhuyād[\hu] r̥cām eva tad rasa3na^r̥cām vīrya3na^r̥cām yajnasya viristam samdadhāti[sam\dhā] (Chū4.17.4)

om / atha yad idam asmin brahma.pura7 daharam pundarīkam veśman1 daharas'asminn antar.ākāśas tasmin yad antar^tad anvestavyam[anu\is] tad vāva vijijnāsitavyam[vi\jnā] iti (Chū8.1.1)

ta ime satyāh kāmā anr̥ta.apidhānās tesām satyānām satām anr̥tam apidhānam yas^yas^asya^itah praiti[pra\i] na tam iha darśanāya \labhate (Chū8.3.1)

atha yat sattrāyanam ity ācaksate[ā\caks] brahmacaryam eva tad brahmacarya3na hy eva sata ātmānas trānam vindate[\vind] (Chū8.5.2a)
atha yat^maunam ity ācaksate[ā\caks] brahmacaryam eva tad brahmacarya3na hy eva^ātmānam anuvidya[anu\vind] \manute (Chū8.5.2b)
atha yad anāśakāyanam ity ācaksate[ā\caks] brahmacaryam eva tad esa hy ātmā na \naśyati yam brahmacarya3na^anuvindate[anu\vind] (Chū8.5.3a)
atha yad aranyāyanam ity ācaksate[ā\caks] brahmacaryam eva tad araś ca ha vai nyaś ca^arnavau brahma.loka7 tr̥tīyasya^mitas^divi[dyaus] - (Chū8.5.3b)
tad airam madīyam saras tad aśvattah somaṣavanas tad aparājitā pūr brahmanas prabhu.vimitam[vi\mā] hiranmayam (Chū8.5.3c)
tad ya eva^etāv aram ca nyam ca^arvanau brahma.loka7 brahmacarya3na^anuvindanti[anu\vind] tesām eva^esa brahma.lokas tesām sarva7su loka7su kāma.cāras^bhavati (Chū8.5.4)

atha ya etā hr̥dayasya nādī1p tāh pingalasya^animan5 tisthanti[\sthā] śuklasya nīlasya pītasya lohitasya^ity (Chū8.6.1a)
asau vā ādityah pingala esa śukla esa nīla esa pīta esa lohitah (Chū8.6.1b)
tad yathā mahā.patha ātata ubhau grāmau gacchati^imam ca^amum ca^evam eva^etā ādityasya raśmi1p ubhau lokau gacchanti[\gam]^imam ca^amum ca - (Chū8.6.2a)
amusmād ādityāt pratāyante[pra\tan] tā āsu nādīsu sr̥ptā[\sr̥p] ābhyas^nādībhyah pratāyante[pra\tan] te'amusminn āditya7 sr̥ptāh[\sr̥p] (Chū8.6.2b)
tad yatra^etat suptah[\svap] samastah samprasannah[sampra\sad] svapnam na vijānāty[vi\jnā] āsu tadā nādīsu sr̥ptas[\sr̥p]^bhavati tam na kaścana pāpman1 spr̥śati[\spr̥ś] tejasā hi tadā sampannas[sam\pad]^bhavati (Chū8.6.3)
atha yatra ^etad abalimānam[abaliman] nītas^bhavati tam abhita āsīnā[\ās] āhur[\ah] jānāsi[\jnā] mām jānāsi mām iti (Chū8.6.4a)
sa yāvad asmāt^śarīrād anutkrāntas[ut\kram]^bhavati tāvat^jānāti[\jnā] (Chū8.6.4b)
atha yatra^etad asmāt^śarīrād utkrāmaty[ut\kram] atha^etair eva raśmibhir ūrdhvam ākramate[ā\kram] sa om iti vā hodvā[ha^ut^vā?] mīyate[\mā/\mi?] (Chū8.6.5a)
sa yāvat ksipyet[\ksip]^manas tāvad ādityam gacchaty[\gam] etad vai khalu lokaḍvāram vidusām prapadanam nirodhas^avidusām (Chū8.6.5b)
tad esa ślokah / śatam ca^ekā ca hr̥dayasya nādī1p tāsām mūrdhan2 abhinihsr̥tā[abhinis\sr̥]^ekā (Chū8.6.6a)
tayā^ūrdhvam āyann[ā\i] amr̥tatvam eti[\i] visvann[visvanc] anyā utkramana7 bhavanty utkramana7 bhavanti (Chū8.6.6b)

ya ātmā^apahata.pāpman1 vijaras^vimr̥tyur viśokas^vijighatso^apipāsah satya.kāmah satyaṣamkalpah so^anvestavyah[anu\is] (Chū8.7.1a)
sa vijijnāsitavyah[vi\jnā] sa sarvāmś ca lokān āpnoti[\āp] sarvāmś ca kāmān yas tam ātmānam anudivya[anu\vid] vijānāti[vi\jnā]^iti ha prajāpatir uvāca (Chū8.7.1b)
tadd ha^ubhaya1d deva.asurā anububudhire[anu\budh] te ha^ūcur[\vac] hanta tam ātmānam anicchāmas[anu\is]^yam ātmānam anvisya[anu\is] sarvāmś ca lokān \āpnoti sarvāmś ca kāmān iti (Chū8.7.2a) [$$]
indras^ha^eva devānām abhipravavrāja[abhipra\vraj] virocanas'asurānām tau ha^asamvidānāv[sam\vid] eva samidh.pānī prajāpatiṣakāśam āgagmatuh[ā\gam] (Chū8.7.2b)
tau ha dvātrimśatam varsāni brahmacaryam ūsatus[\vas] tau ha prajāpatir uvāca[\vac] kim icchan[\is] tāv avāstam[\vas] iti (Chū8.7.3a)
tau ha^ūcatur[\vac] ya ātmā^apahata.pāpman1 vijaras^vimr̥tyur viśokas^vijighatso^apipāsah satya.kāmah satyaṣamkalpah so^anvestavyah (Chū8.7.3b)
sa vijijnāsitavyah[vi\jnā] sa sarvāmś ca lokān \āpnoti sarvāmś ca kāmān yas tam ātmānam anuvidya[anu\vid] vijānāti[vi\jnā]^iti bhagavah^vacas^vedayante[\vid] tam icchan[\is] tāv avāstam[\vas] iti (Chū8.7.3c)
tau ha prajāpatir uvāca[\vac] ya eso^aksini purusas^dr̥śyata[\dr̥ś] esa ātmā^iti ha^uvāca^etad amr̥tam abhayam etad brahma^ity (Chū8.7.4a)
atha yas^ayam bhagavah'apsu parikhyāyate[pari\khyā] yaś ca^ayam ādarśa7 katama esa ity esa u eva^esu sarva7sv anta7sv parikhyāyata[pari\khyā] iti ha^uvāca[\vac] (Chū8.7.4b)
uda.śarāva ātmānam aveksya[ava\īks] yad ātmanas^na vijānīthas[vi\jnā] tan me prabrūtam[pra\brū] iti (Chū8.8.1a)
tau ha^uda.śarāva7'aveksām.cakrāte[ava\īks] tauha prajāpatir uvāca[\vac] kim \paśyatha iti (Chū8.8.1b)
tau ha^ūcatuh sarvam eva^idam āvām bhagavah^ātmānam \paśyāva ā loman.bhya ā nakha5bhyah prtirūpam iti (Chū8.8.1c)
tau ha prajāpatir uvāca[\vac] sādhu.alamkr̥tau suvasanau pariskr̥tau bhūtvā[\bhū]^uda.śarāva7'aveksethām[ava\īks] iti (Chū8.8.2a)
tau ha sādhu.alamkr̥tau suvasanau pariskr̥tau bhūtvā[\bhū]^uda.śarāva7'aveksām.cakrāte[ava\īks] tau ha prajāpatir uvāca kim \paśyatha iti (Chū8.8.2b)
tau ha^ūcatur yathā^eva^idam āvām bhagavah sādhu.alamkr̥tau suvasanau pariskr̥tau sv evam eva^imau bhagavah sādhu.alamkr̥tau suvasanau pariskr̥tāv ity (Chū8.8.3a)
esa ātmā^iti ha^uvāca^etad amr̥tam abhayam etad brahma^iti tau ha śāntaḥr̥dayau pravavrajatuh[pra\vraj] (Chū8.8.3b)
tau ha^anvīksya[anu\īks] prajāpatir uvāca[\vac]^anupalabhya[upa\labh]^ātmānam ananuvidya[anu\vid] vrajatas[\vraj] (Chū8.8.4a)
yatara etad upanisadas^bhavisyanti[\bhū] devā vā^asurā vā te parābhavisyanti[parā\bhū]^iti (Chū8.8.4b)
sa ha śāntaḥr̥daya eva virocanas'asurān jagāma[\gam] tebhyas^ha^etām upanisadam ha^uvāca (Chū8.8.4c)
ātmā^eva^iha mahayya[\mah] ātmā paricarya ātmānam eva^iha \mahayann ātmānam paricarann[pari\car] ubhau lokāv avāpnoti[ava\āp]^imam ca^amum ca^iti (Chū8.8.4d)
tasmād apy adya^iha^adadānam[\dā] aśradddhānam[śrad\dhā] ayajamānam[\yaj] āhur[\ah] āsuras^ bata^ity (Chū8.8.5a)
asurānām hy esā^upanisat pretasya śarīram bhiksā3 vasana3na^alamkāra3na^iti samskurvanty[sam\kr̥] etena hy amum lokam jesyantas[\ji]^\manyante (Chū8.8.5b)
atha ha^indras'aprāpya[pra\āp]^eva devān etad bhayam dadarśa[\dr̥ś] yathā^eva khalu^ayam asmin^śarīra7 sādhu.alamkr̥ta7 sādhu.alamkr̥tas bhavati suvasana7 suvasanah pariskr̥ta7 pariskr̥ta - (Chū8.9.1a)
evam eva^ayam asmin^andha7'andhas^bhavati srāma7 srāmah parivr̥kna7 parivr̥knas'asya^eva śarīrasya nāśam anu^esa naśyati[\naś] na^aham atra bhogyam \paśyāmi^iti (Chū8.9.1b)
sa samidh.pānih punar eyāya[\i] tam ha prajāpatir uvāca[\vac] maghavat8 yat^śāntaḥr̥dayah prāvrājīh[pra\vraj] sārdham virocana3na kim icchan[\is] punar āgama[ā\gam] iti (Chū8.9.2a)
sa ha^uvāca tathā^eva khalu^ayam bhagavah^asmin^śarīra7 sādhu.alamkr̥ta7 sādhu.alamkr̥tas^bhavati suvasana7 suvasanah pariskr̥ta7 pariskr̥ta - (Chū8.9.2b)
evam eva^ayam asmin^andha7'andhas^bhavati srāma7 sramah parivrkna7 parivr̥knas'asya^eva śarīrasya nāśam anu^eva \naśyati na^aham atra bhogyam \paśyāmi^iti (Chū8.9.2c) [atm]
evam eva^esa maghavat8^iti ha^uvāca[\vac]^etam tv eva te bhūyas^anuvyākhyāsyāmi[anuvyā\khyā] (Chū8.9.3a)
vasa[\vas]^aparāni dvatrimśatam varsāni^iti sa ha^aparāni dvātrimśatam varsāny uvāsa[\vas] tasmai ha^uvāca (Chū8.9.3b)

ya esa svapna7 mahīyamānaś[\mah] caranty[\car] esa ātmā^iti ha^uvāca^etad amr̥tam abhayam etad brahma^iti (Chū8.10.1a)
sa ha śāntaḥr̥dayah pravavrāja[pra\vraj] sa ha^aprāpya[pra\āp]^eva devān etad bhayam dadarśa[\dr̥ś] - (Chū8.10.1b)
tad yady api^idam śarīram andham bhavaty anandhah sa bhavati yadi srāmam asrāmas^na^eva^eso^asya dosa3na \dusyati (Chū8.10.1c)
na vadha3na^asya \hanyate na^asya srāmya3na sramas^ghnanti[\han] tv eva^enam vicchādayanti[vi\chad]^iva - (Chū8.10.2a)
apriya.vettr̥1^iva bhavaty api roditi[\rud] iva na^ām atra bhogyam paśyāmi[\paś]^iti (Chū8.10.2b)
sa samidh.pānih punar eyāya[\i] tam ha prajāpatir uvāca maghavat8 pracchānta[praśānta?]ḥr̥dayah pravrājīh[pra\vraj] kim icchan[\is] punar āgama[ā\gam] iti (Chū8.10.3a)
sa ha^uvāca tad yady api^idam bhagavah śarīram andham bhavaty anandhah sa bhavati yadi srāmam asrāmas na^eva^eso^asya dosa3na \dusyati (Chū8.10.3b)
na vadha3na^asya \hanyate na\asya srāmya3na srāmas^ghnanti[\han] tv eva^enam vicchādayanti[vi\chad]^iva^apriya.vettr̥1^iva bhavaty api roditi[\rud]^iva (Chū8.10.4a)
na aham atra bhogyam \paśyāmi^ity evam eva^esa maghavat8^iti ha^uvāca[\vac] (Chū8.10.4b)
etam tv eva te bhūyas^anuvyākhyāsyāmi[anuvyā\khyā] vasa[\vas]^aparāni dvātrimśatam varsāni^iti (Chū8.10.4c)
sa ha^aparāni dvātrimśatam varsāny uvāsa[\vas] tasmai ha^uvāca(Chū8.10.4d)
tad yatra^etat suptah[\svap] samastah samprasannah[sampra\sad] svapnam na vijānāty[vi\jnā] esa ātmā^iti ha^uvāca^etad amr̥tam abhayam etad brahma^iti  (Chū8.11.1a)
sa ha śāntaḥr̥dayah pravavrāja[pra\vraj] sa ha^aprāpya[pra\āp]^eva devān etad bhayam dadarśa[\dr̥ś] (Chū8.11.1b)
na^aha khalu^ayam evam samprati^ātmānam jānāty[\jnā] ayam aham asmi^iti na^u^eva^imāni bhūtāni vināśam eva^apītas[api\i]^bhavati na^aham atra bhogyam \paśyāmi^iti (Chū8.11.1c)
sa samidh.pānih punar eyāya[\i] tam ha prajāpatir uvāca maghavat8 yat^śāntaḥr̥dayah pravrājīh[pra\vraj] kim icchan[\is] punar āgama[ā\gam] iti (Chū8.11.2a)
sa ha^uvāca na^aha khalu^ayam bhagavah^evam samprati^ātmānam jānāty\[\jnā] ayam aham asmi^iti - (Chū8.11.2b)
na^u^evam imāni bhūtāni vināśam eva^apītas[api\ita]^bhavati na^aham atra bhogyam \paśyāmi^iti (Chū8.11.2c)
evam eva^esa maghavat8^iti ha^uvāca[\vac]^etam tv eva te bhūyas^anuvyākhyāsyāmi[anuvyā\khyā] - (Chū8.11.3a)
nas^eva^anyatra^etasmād vasa[\vas]^aparāni panca varsāni^iti sa ha^aparāni panca varsāny uvāsa[\vas] (Chū8.11.3b)
tāny eka.śatam sampedur[sam\pad] etat tad yad āhur[\ah] eka.śatam ha vai varsāni maghavat1 prajāpati7 brahmacaryam uvāsa[\vas] tasmai ha^uvāca (Chū8.11.3c)
maghavat8 martyam vā idam śarīram āttam[ā\dā] mr̥tyunā tad asya^amr̥tasya aśarīrasya^ātmanas'adhisthānam (Chū8.12.1a) [$adhisthāna][atm]
āttas[ā\dā]^vai saśarīrah priya.apriyābhyām na vai saśarīrasya satah priya.apriyayor apahatir asty aśarīram vāva santam na priya.apriya1d spr̥śatah (Chū8.12.1b)
aśarīras^vāyur abhram vidyut stanayitnur aśarīrāny etāni (Chū8.12.2a)
tad yathā^etāny amusmād ākāśāt samutthāya[samut\sthā] param jyotis^upasampadya[upasam\pad] sva3na rūpa3na^abhinispadyante[abhinis\pad] (Chū8.12.2b)
evam eva^esa samprasādas'asmāt^śarīrāt samutthāya[samut\sthā] param jyotis^upasampadya[upasam\pad] sva3na rūpa3na^abhinispadyate[abhinis\pad] sa uttama.purusah (Chū8.12.3a)
sa tatra paryeti[pari\i] jaksat[\jaks] krīdan[\krīd] \ramamānah strībhir vā yānair vā jnātibhir vā na^upajanam smaran[\smr̥]^idam śarīram (Chū8.12.3b)
sa yathā prayogya ācarana7 yukta evam eva^ayam asmin^śarīra7 prānas^yuktah (Chū8.12.3c)
atha yatra^etad ākāśam anuvisannam[anuvi\sanj] caksus^sa cāksusah purusah^carśanāya caksus. (Chū8.12.4a)
atha yas^veda[\vid]^idam jighrāni[\ghrā]^iti sa ātmā gandhāya ghrānam (Chū8.12.4b)
atha yas^veda[\vid]^idam \manvāni^iti sa ātmā manas'asya daivam caksus^sa vā esa etena daiva3na caksusā manasā^etān kāmān \paśyan \ramate, ya ete brahma.loka7 (Chū8.12.5)
tam vā etam devā ātmānam upāsate[upa\ās] tasmāt tesām sarva1p ca lokā āttāh[ā\dā] sarva1p ca kāmāh (Chū8.12.6a)
sa sarvāmś ca lokān \āpnoti savāmś ca kāmān yas tam ātmānam anuvidya[anu\vid] vijānāti[vi\nā]^iti ha prajāpatir uvāca prajāpatir uvāca (Chū8.12.6b)
śyāmāt^śabalam prapadya[pra\pad] śabalāt^śyāmam prapadye[pra\pad]'asva iva romāni vidhūya[vi\dhū] pāpam candra iva rāhu6 mukhāt pramucya[pra\muc] (Chū8.13.1b)
\dhūtvā śarīram akr̥tam kr̥ta.ātmā brahma.lokam abhisambhavāmi[abhisam\bhū]^ity abhisambhavāmi^iti (Chū8.13.1c)
ākāśas^vai nāma nāmar̥ūpayor nirvahitr̥1[nis\vah] te yad antarā tad brahma tad amr̥tam sa ātmā (Chū8.14.1a)
prajājpati6 sabhām veśma prapadye[pra\pad] yaśas'aham bhavāmi brāhmanānām yaśas^rājan6p yaśas^viśām yaśas'aham anuprāpatsi[anupra\pad] (Chū8.14.1b)
sa ha^aham yaśasām yaśas^śyetam adatkam adatkam śyetam lindu mā^abhigām[abhi\gā] lindu mā^abhigām (Chū8.14.1c)

tadd ha^etad brahmā prajāpati4 uvāca[\vac] prajāpatir manu5 manuh prajābhya ācārya.kulād vedam adhītya[adhi\i] yathā.vidhānam guru6 karma.atiśesa3na^abhisamāvr̥tya[abhisamā\vr̥] - (Chū8.15.1a)
kutumba7[kutunba] śuci7 deśa7 svādhyāyam adhīyānas[adhi\i] dhārmikān vidadhad[vi\dhā] (Chū8.15.1b)
ātmani sarva.indriyāni sampratisthāpya[samprati\sthā]^ahimsan[\hims] sarva.bhūtāny anyatra tīrtha5bhyah (Chū8.15.1c)
sa khalu^evam vartayan[\vr̥t] yāvat.āyusam brahma.lokam abhisampadyate[abhisam\pad] na ca punar āvartate[ā\vr̥t] na ca punar āvartate (Chū8.15.1d) =End fo Chāndogya ūpanīshad=


<ṭaittirīya ūpanishad>(ṭū)
om / śam nas^mitrah śam varunah / śam nas^bhavatu^aryaman1 / śam na indras^br̥haspatih / śam nas^visnur uru.kramah / namas^brahmane / namas te vāyu8 (ṭū1.1a)
tvam eva pratyaksam brahma^asi[\as] / tvām eva pratyaksam brahma \vadisyāmi / r̥tam \vadisyāmi / satyam \vadisyāmi (ṭū1.1b)
tat^mām \avatu / tad vaktr̥2 \avatu / \avatu mām / avatu vaktr̥2 / om śāntih śāntih śāntih (ṭū1.1c)

om śiksām vyākhyāsyāmah[vyā\khyā] / varnah svarah / mātrā balam / sāma samtānah / ity uktah śiksā.adhyāyah (ṭū1.2)

saha nau yaśas. / saha nau brahma.varcasam / atha^atah samhitāyā upanisadam vyākhyāsyāmah[vyā\khyā] (ṭū1.3.1a)
pancasv adhikarana7su / adhilokam adhijyautisam adhividyam adhiprajam adhyātmam (ṭū1.3.1b)
tā mahāṣamhitā ity ācaksate[ā\caks] / atha^adhilokam / pr̥thivī pūrvar̥ūpam / dyaus^uttarar̥ūpam / ākāśah samdhih (ṭū1.3.1c)

vāyuh samdhānam / ity adhilokam / atha^adhijyautisam / agnih pūrvar̥ūpam / āditya uttarar̥ūpam / āpas^samdhih / vaidyutah samdhānam / ity adhijyautisam (ṭū1.3.2a)
atha^adhividyam / ācāryah pūrvar̥ūpam (ṭū1.3.2b)
antevāsin1 uttarar̥ūpam / vidyā samdhih / pravacanam samdhānam / ity adhividyam (ṭū1.3.3a)
atha^adhiprajam / mātr̥1 pūrvar̥ūpam / pitr̥1^uttarar̥ūpam / prajā samdhih / prajananam samdhānam / ity adhiprajam (ṭū1.3.3b)
atha^adhyātmam / adharā hanuh pūrvar̥ūpam / uttarā hanur uttarar̥ūpam / vāc^samdhih / jihvā samdhanam / ity adhyātmam (ṭū1.3.4a)
iti^imā mahāṣamhitāh / ya evam etām mahāṣamhitā vyākhyātā[vyā\kyā] veda[\vid] / samdhīyate[sam\dhā] prajayā paśubhih / brahma.varcasa3na^anna.adya3na suvargya3na loka3na (ṭū1.3.4b)

yaś chandasām r̥sabhas^viśvar̥ūpah / chandas.bhyas^adhy amr̥tāt sambabhūva[sam\bhū] sa mā^indras^madhā3 spr̥notu[\spr̥] (ṭū1.4.1a)
amr̥tasya deva dhāranas^bhūyāsam[\bhū] / śarīram me vicarsanam / jihvā me madhumattamā (ṭū1.4.1b)
karnābhyām bhūri viśruvam[vi\śru] / brahmanah kośas'asi medha3 pihitah[pi\dhā/api\dhā] (ṭū1.4.1c)
śrutam me gopāya / āvahantī[ā\vah] vitanvānā[vi\tan] (ṭū1.4.1d)
kurvānā[\kr̥]'acīram[ciram/aciram?] ātmanah / vāsas1p mama go1p ca / anna.pāna1d ca sarvadā (ṭū1.4.2a)
tatas^me śrī2 āvaha[ā\vah] / lomaśām paśubhih saha svāhā / ā mā yantu[\i] brahmacārinah svāhā (ṭū1.4.2b)
vi mā^āyantu[? vyā\i] brahmacārinah svāhā / pra mā^āyantu[?prā\i] brahmacarinah svāhā / damāyantu[\dam?] brahmacārinah svāhā / śamāyantu[\śam?] brahmacārinah svāhā (ṭū1.4.2c)
yaśas^jana7'asāni[\as] svāhā / śreyas1m vasyaso^asāni[\as] / tam tvā bhaga praviśāni[pra\viś] svāhā (ṭū1.4.3a)
sa mā bhaga praviśa[pra\viś] svāhā / tasmint sahasra.śākha7 / ni bhaga^aham tvayi mr̥je[\mr̥j] svāhā (ṭū1.4.3b)
yathā^āpas^pravatā yanti[\i] / yathā māsā ahar jaram[?] / evam mām brahmacārinah / dhātr̥8 āyantu[ā\i] sarvatah svāhā (ṭū1.4.3c)
prativeśas'asi[\as] pra mā bhāhi[pra\bhā] pra mā padyasva[pra\pad] (ṭū1.4.3d)

bhūr bhuvar^suvas[!]^iti vā etās tisras^vyāhr̥ti1p / tāsām u ha sma^etām caturthīm / māhācamasyah pravedayate[pra\vid] (ṭū1.5.1a)
mahas^iti / tad brahma sa ātmā / angāny anyā devatāh (ṭū1.5.1b)
bhūr iti vā ayam lokah / bhuvar^ity antariksam / suvas^ity asau lokah (ṭū1.5.1c)
mahas^ity ādityah / āditya3na vāva sarva1p lokā \mahīyante / bhūr iti vā agnih / bhuvar^iti vāyuh / suvas^ity ādityah (ṭū1.5.2a)
mahas^iti candramas1 / candramasā vāva sarvāni jyotis1p \mahīyante / bhūr iti vā r̥cah / bhuvar^iti sāmāni / suvas^iti yajus1p (ṭū1.5.2b)
mahas^iti brahma / brahmanā vāva sarva1p vedā \mahīyante / bhūr iti vai prānah / bhuvar^ity apānah / suvas^iti vyānah (ṭū1.5.3a)
mahas^ity annam / anna3na vāva sarva1p prānā \mahīyante / tā vā etāś catasraś caturdhā (ṭū1.5.3b)
catasraś catasras^vyāhr̥ti1p / tā yo veda[\vid] / sa veda brahma / sarva1p'asmai devā balim āvahanti[ā\vah] (ṭū1.5.3c)

sa ya eso^antarḥr̥daya ākāśah / tasminn ayam purusas^manasṃayah / amr̥tas^hiranmayah (ṭū1.6.1a)
antara3na tāluka1d ya esa stana iva^avalambate[ava\lamb] / sā^indra.yonih (ṭū1.6.1b)
yatra^asau keśa.antas^vivartate[vi\vr̥t] / vyapohya[vyapa\vah] śīrka.kapāla7 / bhūr ity agni7 pratitisthati[prati\sthā] / bhuvar iti vāyu7 (ṭū1.6.1b)
suvas^ity āditya7 / mahas^iti brahmani / āpnoti[\āp] svārājyam / \āpnoti manasas.patim / vākpatiś[vāc.pati] caksus.patih / śrotra.patir vijnāna.patih (ṭū1.6.2a)
etat tatas^bhavati / ākāśa.śarīram brahma / satya.ātma prāna.ārāmam manas.ānandam / śāntiṣamr̥ddham amr̥tam / iti prācīnayogya^upāssva[upa\ās] (ṭū1.6.2b)

pr̥thivī^antariksam dyaus^diśas'avāntaraḍiśāh / agnir vāyur ādityaś candramas1 naksatrāni / āpas^osadhi1p vanaspati1p ākāśa ātmā / ity adhidaivatam (ṭū1.7.1a)
atha^adhyātmam / prānas^vyānas'apāna udānah samānah / caksus^śrotram manas^vāc^tvac. / carma māmsam snāvā[?]^asthi majjā - (ṭū1.7.1b)
etad adhividhāya[adhivi\dhā] r̥sir avocat[\vac] / pānktam vā idam sarvam / pānkta3na^eva pānktam spr̥noti[\spr̥]^iti (ṭū1.7.1c) [atm]

om iti brahma / om iti^idam sarvam / om ity etad anukr̥tir ha sma vā apy o śrāvaye[\śru]^ity āśravayanti[ā\śru] (ṭū1.7.1a)
om iti sāmāni gāyanti[\gai] / om śom iti śastrāni \śamsanti / om ity adhvaryuh pratigaram pratigr̥nāti[prati\gr̥] / om iti brahmā prasautu[pra\su] (ṭū1.7.1b)
om ity agnihotram anujānāti[anu\jnā] / om iti brāhmanah pravaksyann[pra\vac] āha[\ah] brahma^upāpnuvāni[upa\āp]^iti / brahma^eva^upāpnoti[upa\āp] (ṭū1.7.1c)

r̥tam ca svādhyāya.pravacana1d ca / satyam ca svādhyāya.pravacana1p ca / tapas^ca svādhyāya.pravacana1d ca / damaś ca svādhyāya.pravacana1d ca(ṭū1.9.1a)
śamaś ca svādhyāya.pravacana1d ca / agni1p ca svādhyāya.pravacana1d ca / agnihotram ca svadhyāya.pravacana1d ca (ṭū1.9.1b)

prajanaś ca svādhyāya.pravacana1d ca / prajāatiś ca svādhyāya.pravacana1d ca (ṭū1.9.1d)
satyam iti satya.vacas1 rāthītarah / tapas^iti tasṇityah pauruśistih / svādhyāya.pravacana1d eva^iti nākas^maudgalyah / tadd hi tapas tadd hi tapas. (ṭū1.9.1e)

aham vr̥ksasya rerivan1 / kīrtih pr̥tham giri6 iva / ūrdhva.pavitras^vājinī^iva su.amr̥tam asmi (ṭū1.10.1a)
dravinam savarcasam / sumedhā amr̥ta.uksitah / iti triśanku6 veda.anuvacanam (ṭū1.10.1b)
vedam anūcya[anu\vac]^ācāryas^antevāsinam anuśāsti[anu\śās] / satyam \vada / dharmam \cara / svādhyāyān mā pramadah[pra\mad] (ṭū1.11.1a)
ācāryāya priyam dhanam āhr̥tya[ā\hr̥]  prajāṭantum mā vyavacchetsīh[vyava\chid] (ṭū1.11.1b)
satyāt^na pramaditavyam[pra\mad] / svādhyāya.pravacanābhyām na pramaditavyam (ṭū1.11.1c)
deva.pitr̥.kāryābhyām na pramaditavyam[pra\mad] / mātr̥ḍevas^bhava / pitr̥ḍevas^bhava / ācāryaḍevas^bhava / atithiḍevas^bava (ṭū1.11.2a)
yāny anavadyāni karmāni / tāni sevitavyāni[\sev]  na^u itarāni / yāny asmākam su.caritāni / tāni tvayā^upāsyāni[upa\ās] (ṭū1.11.2b)
na^u itarāni / ye ke ca^asmat^śreyāmsas^brāhmanāh / tesām tvayā^āsana3na praśvasitavyam[pra\śvas] / śraddhā3 deyam[\dā] / aśraddha3'adeyam[\dā] / (ṭū1.11.3a)
śrī3 deyam / hrī3 deyam / bhī3 deyam / samvidā deyam / atha yadi te karma.vicikitsā vā vr̥tta.vicikitsa vā syāt[\as] (ṭū1.11.3b)
ye tatra brāhmanāh sammarśinah / yuktā[\yuj] āyuktāh[ā\yuj] / alūksā dharma.kāmāh syuh[\as] / yatha te tatra varteran[\vr̥t] / tathā tatra vartethāh[\vr̥t] (ṭū1.11.4a)
atha^abhyākhyāta7su[abhyā\khyā] / ye tatra brāhmanāh sammarśinah / yuktā[\yuj] āyuktāh[ā\yuj] / alūksā dharma.kāmāh syuh[\as] (ṭū1.11.4b)
yathā te tesu varteran[vr̥t] / tathā tesu vartethāh[\vr̥t] / esa ādeśah / esa upadeśah /esā veda.upanisat (ṭū1.11.4c)
etad anuśāsanam / evam upāsitavyam[upa\ās] / evam u ca^etad upāsyam[upa\ās] (ṭū1.11.4d)

śan nas^mitrah śam varunah / śam nas^bhavatv aryaman1 / śam na indras^br̥haspatih / śam nas^visnur uru.kramah (ṭū1.12.1a)
namas^brahmane / namas te vāyu8 / tvam eva jpratyaksam brahma^asi[\as] / tvām eva pratyaksam brahma^avādisam[\vad] / r̥tam avādisam[\vad] satyam avadisam[\vad] (ṭū1.12.1b)
tat^mām āvīt[\av] / tad vaktr̥2 āvīt[\av] / āvīt^mām / āvīt^vaktr̥2 / om śāntih śāntih śāntih (ṭū1.12.1)

om brahmavit^\āpnoti param / tad esā^abhyuktā[abhi\vac] / satyam jnānam anantam brahma / yas^veda[\vid] nihitam[ni\dhā] guhāyām parama5 vyoman / so^\aśunute sarvān kānān saha / brahmanā vipaścitā^iti (ṭū2.1a)
tasmād vā etasmād ātmana ākāśah sambhūtah[sam\bhū] / ākāśād vāyuh / vāyu5 agnih / agni5 āpas. / ap.bhyah pr̥thivī / pr̥thivī5 osadhi1p / osadhī.bhyas^annam / annāt purusah (ṭū2.1b)
sa vā esa puruso^annar̥asamayah / tasya^idam eva śiras. / ayam daksinah paksah / ayam uttarah paksah / ayam ātmā / idam puccham pratisthā / tad apy esa ślokas bhavati (ṭū2.1c)

annād vai prajāh prajāyante[pra\jan] / yāh kāś ca pr̥thivīm śritāh / atha anna3na^eva jīvanti[\jīv] (ṭū2.2a)
atha^enad api yanty[\i] antatah / annam hi bhūtānām jyestham / tasmāt sarva.ausadham ucyate[\vac] / sarvam vai te'annam \āpnuvanti / ye'annam brahma^upasate[upa\ās] (ṭū2.2b)
annam hi bhūtānām jyestham / tasmat sarva.ausadham ucyate[\vac] / annād bhūtāni jāyante[\jan] / jātāny anna3na vardhante[\vr̥dh] (ṭū2.2c)
\adyate'\atti ca bhūtāni tasmād annam tad ucyate[\vac] iti / tasmād vā etasmād annar̥asam ayāt[\i] (ṭū2.2d)
anyas^antara ātmā prānamayah / tena^esa pūrnah / sa vā esa prusa.vidha eva / tasya purusa.vidhatām / anu^ayam purusa.vidhah (ṭū2.2e)
tasya prāna eva śiras. / vyānas^daksinah paksah / apana uttarah paksah / ākāśa ātmā / pr̥thivī puccham pratisthā / tad apy esa ślokas^bhavati (ṭū2.2f)

prānam devā anu prānanti[anupra\an] / manusyāh paśu1p ca ye / prānas^hi bhūtānām āyus. / tasmāt sarva.āyusam ucyate[\vac] (ṭū2.3a)
sarvam eva ta āyus^yanti[\i] / ye prānam brahma^upāsate[upa\ās] / prānas^hi bhūtānām āyus. (ṭū2.3b)
tasmāt sarva.āyusam ucyate[\vac] iti / tasya^esa eva śārīra ātmā / yah pūrvasya / tasmād vā etasmāt prānamayāt (ṭū2.3c) [atm]
anyas^antara ātmā manasṃayah / tena^esa pūrnah / sa vā esa purusa.vidha eva / tasya purusa.vidhatām / anu^ayam prusa.vidhah / (ṭū2.3d)
tasya yajus^eva śiras. / r̥c^daksinah paksah / sāma^uttarah paksah / ādeśa ātmā / atharva.angirasah puccham pratisthā / tad apy esa ślokas^bhavati (ṭū2.3e)

yatas^vācas nivartante[ni\vr̥t] / aprāpya[pra\āp] manasā saha / ānandam brahmanas^vidvat1m / na bibheti[\bhī] kadācana^iti (ṭū2.4a)
tasya^esa eva śārīra ātmā / yah pūrvasya / tasmād vā etasmāt^manasṃayāt (ṭū2.4b)
anyas^antara ātmā vijnānamayah / tena^esa pūrnah / sa vā esa purusa.vidha eva / tasya purusa.vidhatām / anu^ayam purusa.vidhah (ṭū2.4c)
tasya śraddhā eva śiras. / r̥tam daksinah paksah / satyam uttarah paksah / yoga ātmā / mahas^puccham pratisthā / tad apy esa ślokas^bhavati (ṭū2.4d)

vijnānam yajnam \tanute / karmāni \tanute'api ca / vijnānam devāh sarva1p / brahma jyestham upāsate[upa\ās] (ṭū2.5a)
vijnānam brahma ced veda[\vid] / tasmāt^cet^na pramādyati[pra\mad] / śarīra7 pāpmanas^hitvā / sarvān kāmānt samaśnuta[sam\aś] iti (ṭū2.5b)
tasya^esa eva śārīra ātmā / yah pūrvasya / tasmād vā etasmād vijnānamayāt (ṭū2.5c)
anyas^antara ātmā^ānandamayah / tena^esa pūrnah / sa vā esa purusa.vidha eva / tasya purusa.vidhatām / anu^ayam purusa.vidhah (ṭū2.5d)
tasya priyam eva śiras. / modas^daksinah paksah / pramoda uttarah paksah / ānanda ātmā / brahma puccham pratisthā / tad apy esa ślokas^bhavati (ṭū2.5e)

asann[\as] eva sa bhavati / asat^brahma^iti veda[\vid] cet / asti brahma^iti ced veda[\vid] / santam[sat] enam tatas^vidur[\vid] iti(ṭū2.(ṭū2.6a)
tasya^esa eva śārīra ātmā / yah pūrvasya atha^atas'anupraśnāh / uta^avidvat1m amum lokam pretya[pra\i] / kaścana gaccatī3 / āho vidvat1m amum lokam pretya[pra\i] (ṭū2.6b)
kaścit samaśnutā3[sam\aś] u / so^akāmayata[\kam] / bahu syām[\as] prajāyeta[pra\jan]^iti / sa tapas^atapyata[\tap] idam sarvam asr̥jata[\sr̥j] (ṭū2.6c)
yad idam kimca / tat sr̥stvā[\sr̥j] / tad eva^anuprāviśat[anupra\viś] / tad anupraviśya / sat^ca tyat^ca^abhavat[\bhū] (ṭū2.6d) [atm]
niruktam ca^aniruktam ca / nilayam ca^anilayam ca / vijnānam ca^avijnānam ca / satyam ca^anr̥tam ca satyam abhavati[\bhū] (ṭū2.6e)
yat idam kimca / tat satyam abhyācaksate[abhyā\caks] / tad apy esa ślokas^bhavati (ṭū2.6f)

asat^vā idam agra āsīt[\as] / tatas^vai sat^ajāyata[\jan] / tad ātmānam asvayam akuruta[\kr̥] / tasmāt tat sukr̥tam ucyate[\vac] iti (ṭū2.7a)
rasas^vai sah / rasam hy eva^aya labdhvā^ānandin1 bhavati / kas^hy eva^anyāt[\an] kah prānyāt[pra\an] yad esa ākāśa ānandas^na syāt[\as] / esa hy eva^ānandayāti[ā\nand] (ṭū2.7b)
yadā hy eva^esa etasminn adr̥śya7'anātmya7'anirukta7'anilaya7'abhayam pratisthām \vindate / atha so^abhayam gatas^bhavati (ṭū2.7c)
yadā hy^eva^esa etasminn udaram antaram kurute[\kr̥] / atha tasya bhayam bhavati[\bhū] / tat tv eva bhayam vidusas[vidvat]'amanvānasya[\man] / tad apy esa ślokas^bhavati (ṭū2.7d)

bhīsā^asmād vātah pavate[\pū] bhīsā^udeti[ut\i] sūryah / bhīsā^asmād agniś c^indraś ca / pr̥yur dhāvati[\dhāv] pancama iti (ṭū2.8.1a)
sā^esā^ānandasya mīmāmsā bhavati[\bhū] / yuvan1 syāt[\as] sādhu yuvan1^adhyāyakah / āśistas[ā\śās]^dr̥dhisthas^balisthah (ṭū2.8.1b)
tasya^iyam pr̥thivī sarvā vittasya pūrnā syāt / sa ekas mānusa ānandah / te ye śatam mānusā ānandāh (ṭū2.8.1c)
sa ekas^manusya.gandharvānām ānandah / śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya / te ye śatam manusya.gandharvānām ānandāh / sa ekas^deva.gandharvānām ānandah / śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya (ṭū2.8.2a)
te ye śatam deva.gandharvānām ānandāh / sa ekah pitr̥r̥nām cira.loka.lokānām ānandah / śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya (ṭū2.8.2b)
te ye śatam pitr̥r̥nām cira.loka.lokānām ānandāh / sa eka ājāna.jānām devānām ānandah - (ṭū2.8.2c)
śrotriyasya ca^akāmātasya / te ye śatam ājāna.jānām devānām ānandah / sa ekah karmaḍevānām devānām ānandah / ye karmanā devān apiyanti[ap\i] / śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya (ṭū2.8.3a)
te ye śatam karmaḍevānām devānām ānandāh / sa ekas^devānām ānandah / śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya (ṭū2.8.3b)
te ye śatam devānām ānandāh / sa eka indrasya^ānandah - (ṭū2.8.3c)
śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya / te ye śatam indriyasya^ānandāh / sa ekas^br̥haspati6 ānandah / śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya / te ye śatam devānām ānandāh / sa eka indrasya^ānandah - (ṭū2.8.3d)
śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya / te ye śatam indrasya^ānandāh / sa ekas^br̥haspati6 ānandah / śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya (ṭū2.8.4a)
te ye śatam br̥haspati6 ānandāh / sa ekah prajāpati6 ānandah / śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya  (ṭū2.8.4b)
te ye śatam prajāpati6 ānandāh / sa ekas^brahmana ānandah / śrotriyasya ca^akāmaḥatasya (ṭū2.8.4c)
sa yaś ca^ayam purusa7 / yaś ca^aśāv āditya7 / sa ekah / sa ya evamvit/ asmāt^lokāt pretya[pra\i] etam annamayam ātmānam upasamkrāmati[upasam\kram] (ṭū2.8.5a)
etam prānamayam ātmānam upasamkrāmati[upasam\kram] / etam manasṃayam ātmānam upasamkrāmati[upasam\kram] - (ṭū2.8.5b)
etam vijnānamayam ātmānam upasamkrāmati[upasam\kram] etam ānandamayam ātmānam upasamkrāmati[upasam\kram] / tad esa ślokas^bhavati (ṭū2.8.5c)
